reprimand ['reprɪmɑːnd] vt. 训斥；谴责 n. 训斥；谴责 15361

词源: 1630s, from French réprimande (16c.), from Middle French reprimende "reproof," from Latin reprimenda "that is to be repressed" (as in reprimenda culpa "fault to be checked"), fem. singular of reprimendus, gerundive of reprimere "hold back, curb," figuratively "check, confine, restrain, refrain". (from PIE root *per- (4)"to strike"). Spelling influenced in French by mander "to summon."
助记:来自拉丁语 reprimere:指责,申斥
助记:re- (=back, again: 再；重新)+ prim (=press=to press, check, confine: 按压；限制；阻止)+ -and (动词、名词后缀)→ (因某人行为越过既定规范、纪律)重新 (用语言)按压、限制某人的行动；阻止某人的行为 → 训斥；谴责

re- (向后, 往回)+ prim (按；压)+ -and (动名词后缀)→ 训斥；谴责
搭配: reprimand sb (for doing sth.): 因某事训斥某人

a severe reprimand: 严厉的斥责

释义: (VERB)训斥；斥责；谴责

If someone is reprimanded, they are spoken to angrily or seriously for doing something wrong, usually by a person in authority.

![](images/43200c2eb9176d7afe5cc471585e8bb132250693e98ee5c8c5e0dfceccd05dc3.jpg)

训斥:谴责

与 reprimand 同样表达 “责备, 批评” 含义的单词还有 reproach。

词源: mid-14c., "a rebuke, blame, censure;" also "object of scorn or contempt;" c. 1400, as "disgrace, state of disgrace," from Old French reproche "blame, shame, disgrace" (12c.), from reprochier "to blame, bring up against".
助记:re- (=opposite of: 相反)+ proach (=prope =near: 靠近的)→ bring near to: 使接近 →现代含义引申为get in (someone's)face: 贴近某人的脸 →为了责备/批评某人；丢脸
搭配:reproach to sb/sth:(给……)带来羞辱的人(或事)；(使……)丢脸的人(或事)

beyond/above reproach:无可指责

approach sb (for sth/for doing sth)/approach sb (with sth/with doing sth):
因某事责备/批评某人

bring reproach upon herself: 使她很丢面子

![](images/1aec80603b0664874a55a98a218a1da8f23bef2839abb2e905557fc442fd3e3c.jpg)

Print 的基本含义为 “印；印刷”。

词源:Proto-Indo-European root meaning "to strike," an extended sense from root *per- (1)"forward, through."

print [print] vt. 印刷；发表；刊登；印(数字、字母或图案)；冲印；用印刷体书写 n. 印刷；印花布料；印花；冲印出的照片；版画；印刷字；脚印；指印 adi. 印刷的(媒体)2228

词源: c. 1300, "impression, mark" (as by a stamp or seal), from Old French preinte "impression," noun use of fem. past participle of preindre "to press, crush," altered from prembre, from Latin premere "to press, hold fast, cover, crowd, compress" (from PIE root *per- (4)"to strike"). The Old French word also was borrowed into Middle Dutch (prente, Dutch prent)and other Germanic languages.

拉丁语动词premere(按；压)在古法语中派生的过去分词preindre,形成了名词preinte(压印),为英语print的词源。后来引申义有刊印:印花:版画:脚印:印刷的等
搭配:print his own posters:印刷自己的宣传海报

a printing and publishing company: 一家印刷出版公司

the print media: 印刷媒体

in print/get into print: (在书刊或报纸上)发表；刊登

in print: (书)仍在出版

out of print: (书)已经停印

study the fine print of his contract: 研读合同细则

由print组成的单词有printer, printout, imprint, reprint, newsprint, fingerprint, footprint, reprimand 等。

printed ['prɪntɪd] adj. 印刷的；已印好的 7240
助记:print(印刷)+-ed(形容词后缀)→印刷的；已印好的
搭配:printed materials:印刷材料

printer ['prɪntə] n. 打印机；印刷工人；印刷公司 5954
助记:print(印刷)+-er(名词后缀)→打印机；印刷工人；印刷公司
搭配:laser printer:激光印刷机

inkjet printer:喷墨式打印机

send off to the printers:已经寄给印刷厂了

printing [ˈprɪntɪŋ] n. 印刷(术)；(书籍的)一次印刷；印刷体(一种书写方法)7335
助记:print(印刷)+-ing(名词后缀)→印刷术；(书籍的)一次印刷；印刷体
搭配:first printing:首印

the invention of printing:印刷术的发明

the printing industry:印刷业

printout ['prɪntaʊt] n. 打印件 14644
助记: print(印刷)+ -out(从里面往外；出来)→在印刷中从(打印机)里面出来的文件资料→打印件
搭配: a computer printout of various financial projections: 各种财政计划的计算机打印资料

imprint [Im'print] n. 深远影响；印痕 vt. 铭刻；压印 10542
助记: im- (=into, in: 进入；使)+ print (=to press: 按；压)→引申词义印

在里面的一 →深远影响；铭刻；压印
搭配: an indelible imprint: 不可磨灭的影响

imprint sth. on/in/onto sth.: 在……上压印

imprint sth. on your mind/memory/brain etc.: 铭记在心；留在脑海里

imprint with message or logo: 印上信息或标识

![](images/7fcaaeb7d0c0f09976dda1f49b06641742e9d07f7897111c971fc4474b046905.jpg)

压印

reprint [ri:'print] vt. 重印；再版 n. 重印；再版；重印本；再版本 9450
助记:re- (=back, again: 再；重新)+print (印刷；出版)→重印；再版；重印本
搭配: reprint in 1918: 1918年再版

a reprint of a 1962 novel: 1962年小说的重印本

newsprint ['nju:zprint] n. 新闻纸；报纸上的文字；印刷油墨 17353
助记:news(新闻)+print(打印)→用来打印新闻的纸张；(为了报道新闻)在报纸上打印出来的文字；打印新闻用的墨水→新闻纸；报纸上的文字；印刷油墨
搭配: a newsprint warehouse: 一个新闻纸货仓

the acres of newsprint devoted to somebody: 有关某人的大量的文字报道

get their hands covered in newsprint: 手上沾满了油墨

fingerprint ['fɪŋgəprint] n. 指纹 vt. 提取……的指纹；提取在……上的指纹 7396
助记:finger(手指)+print(印痕；印迹)→表示指印；指纹
搭配:his fingerprint on the murder weapon:他留在凶器上的指纹

take someone's fingerprints:让某人按手印

fingerprint the canoe:提取独木舟上的指纹

footprint ['fəutprint] n. 脚印, 足迹; (某物的)占位面积; (通信卫星)覆盖区 8583
助记:foot(脚)+print(印痕；印迹)→脚印；足迹
搭配:footprints in the sand:沙地足迹
the footprints of a deer:一头鹿的足迹
carbon footprint:碳足迹；碳排放量
a 50% smaller footprint:占位面积小50%的

词根“count”表示“计算；数”,同样表示“计算；数”的词根还有“calc-, -ckon, -quant”。

词源: late 14c., "to enumerate, assign numerals to successively and in order; repeat the numerals in order," also "to reckon among, include," from Old French conter "to count, add up," also "tell a story," from Latin computare "to count, sum up, reckon together," from com "with, together" (see com-)+ putare "to reckon," originally "to prune," from PIE root *pau- (2)"to cut, strike, stamp."

Intransitive sense "be of value or worth" is from 1857. Related: Counted; counting. To count on "rely or depend upon" is from 1640s. To count against (transitive)"to be to the disadvantage of" is by 1888. To count (someone)in "consider (someone)a participant or supporter" is from 1857; count (someone)out in the opposite sense "leave out of consideration" is from 1854.

count [kaunt] vi. 数数；有价值 vt. 数……的数目；把……计算在内 vt.&vi. 看作(count/count as)n. 点数；数目；罪状；伯爵 1338

词源:count表示计算。来源于拉丁语computare(计算),传入古法语变为center,其”加起来报账”的含义后来被引申为”讲故事”,这个意义在派生词account和recount中有所体现。

count表示伯爵。来源于法语counte。在古罗马帝国时期,罗马皇帝身边的亲信往往能得到皇帝的宠爱,掌管帝国的军政大权,有时还会出任地方官吏,最常见的是担任某行省的总督。欧洲大陆部分国家的伯爵爵位名称就出自拉丁文的comes,意为“侍从”。例如,法语中表示“伯爵”的单词为counte,出自拉丁文comitem,即comes的宾格,意思就是“伙伴,侍从”,进入英语后演变为英语单词count,表示欧洲大陆地区的伯爵。
助记:来自拉丁语computare,含义为“数数,计算……的总数,一起估算”。

com- (=with, together: 一起; 总共)+put- (=to reckon: 计算)→加起来计算, 数算总数→计算; 把……计算在内; 数目+e→引申义为有价值: 看作
搭配:count on:指望；依赖(=depend on)

count as:算是:看作

keep count of/lose count of: 计其数/无法计其数

例句:When labeling games as violent or non-violent, should a hero eating a ghost really be counted as a violent event?

当标签游戏作为暴力或者非暴力,一个英雄把幽灵吃掉应不应该算得上是一个暴力事件?

![](images/fb59ca510ac7c73936bc07c39c1d0285f0c241e8d1853c23ab71a6b0719acf8f.jpg)

单词 count 的派生词有 discount, recount, counting, countless, counter 等。

discount ['dɪskaʊnt] n. 折扣 vt. 对……打折；不理会 4554
搭配:discount the rumor:不理会这个传闻

recount [rɪ'kaʊnt] vt. 叙述；描述 n. 重新计票 5557
搭配:recount the story:叙述故事
want a recount:要求重新计票

counting ['kauntɪŋ] prep. 算上；把……计算在内 9659
搭配:not counting administrative expenses:不算行政开支
and counting:数量继续增长
more than 100 feet tall and counting:高100多英尺并在继续长高

countless ['kauntlɪs] adj. 数不清的 5115
搭配:countless people:无数人

counter ['kauntə] n. 柜台；(尤指厨房的)工作台；抵消物 vt.&vi. 反驳；抵消；抗衡 2851
搭配: at the checkout counter: 在结账台
counter staff: 柜台职员
over the counter: (买药)不用处方
over-the-counter: 不通过交易所的
as a counter to: 作为……的抵消物; 遏制力量

countertop=worktop ['kauntətap] n. (厨房的)工作台面 13028

countdown ['kaontdaun] n. 倒数计秒；倒计时阶段[+to] 15156
搭配:the countdown to the World Cup 世界杯的倒计时阶段

account [ə'kaunt] n. 账户；客户；账目；报道 1075
助记:ac-(加强语气)+count(数目)→账户；账目(记录钱的数量)

ac+count(计算；数)→计算(所占数量)→占……比例；考虑(“把……计算在内”即“考虑在内”)

ac+count(起作用；有价值)→解释；说明(“某原因起了作用”即“该原因能解释说明问题”)

例句:1)In the US, these groups account for an increasing percentage of the population.

在美国,这些人群数量占总人口比例在急剧增加。

2)This account of yourself is actually a sketch of your working life and should include education, experience and references.

这样一个你自己的描述实际上是你工作生活的一个梗概,应该包括教育背景,工作经验和证明。

3)these changes may account in part for the increased prevalence of obesity.

这些变化部分上可以解释肥胖的流行。

![](images/d4a4d4c096a4073cc559dd12ad0e95073edbba39807605aef48966053cc1db4a.jpg)

仿写例句:根据最新的统计数据,学英文占据了大学生50%的课外时间,这就部分上解释了为什么读经典著作的人越来越少。

According to/By the latest statistics, English learning accounts for/makes up 50 percent of the spare time among college students. This accounts in part for why those who are willing to read classics/classical works are becoming less and less.

![](images/97afbdcc656776fc11410f4de3594d699f68eb3337b80fb9a53bb30b73b08f2c.jpg)

单词account的派生词有accountability, accountable, accountant, accounting 等。

accountability [ə,kaʊntəˈbɪlɪti] n. 有责任 4855
搭配: the accountability of a company's directors to the shareholders: 公司董事向股东所负之责

accountable [ə'kaʊntəb(ə)l] adj. 有有责任的；应作解释的 5795
搭配:should be accountable to their customers:应该对它们的顾客负责

搭配:the accounting firm:会计事务所
a career in accounting:会计职业

词根 “counter-” 表示 “对抗；作对；对面的；对方的”

词源: counter (v.)“go against, come against, engage in combat,” late 14c., short for acountren, encounters. In boxing, “to give a return blow while receiving or parrying a blow from one’s opponent,” by 1861. Related: Countered; countering.

counter (adv.)“contrary, in opposition, in an opposite direction,” mid-15c., from counter- or from Anglo-French and Old French contre “against,” both ultimately from Latin contra (see contra (prep., adv.)). As a preposition, “contrary to, opposite, against,” mid-15c.

counter (adj.)1590s, “acting in opposition,” from counter (adv.)or counter-.

![](images/66f7c2ff65dbb7897893a779d09d32b626d40c14a0f8048bf76189dcb9ad35e4.jpg)

counter的派生词或合成词有counterpart, counteract, encounter, counterattack, counterbalance, counterculture, counterpoint, countertop, counterweight.

encounter [ɪn'kaʊntə; en-] vt. 遭遇；邂逅 n. 邀遇；特殊经历 2736
助记:encounter major and minor stresses:遇到或大或小的压力
a remarkable encounter with:与……的惊人邂逅

搭配:international counterparts:国际上的同龄人；国际同行

搭配:counteract the effect:抵消该影响

counteract his withdrawal symptoms: 消除他的脱瘾症

counterattack ['kauntərətæk] n. 反击；反攻 17580

counterbalance ['kauntə,bæl(ə)ns] vt. 平衡；抵消 n. 平衡因素；制衡力 18511
搭配:add honey to counterbalance the acidity:加点蜂蜜以调和酸味

counterweight=counterbalance. ['kauntəweit] n. 平衡的行动；平衡的建议 20091
搭配:as a useful counterweight to:相对……来说,可作为一个有益的平衡

counterculture ['kaʊntəkʌltʃə] n. 反主流文化 19604
搭配:the counterculture revolution of the late 1960s:20世纪60年代末的反正统文化革命

counterpoint ['kauntəpɔɪnt] n. (音乐)对位法；旋律配合；有趣的对比, 愉意的对照[+to] 14391
搭配: a counterpoint to a professional judgement: 与专家的意见作了有趣的对照

the perfect counterpoint to the peace and quiet of Reims: 与兰斯的平和宁静相比简直是另一番景象

![](images/f92a5c7bd00db3d85ecd74ed8d6b3757a63a35da119c2acaf4252bbd353593f6.jpg)

"compute" 表示 “计算”。

compute [kəm'pju:t] vt.&vi. 计算(结果、答案、总数等)7968

词源:来自拉丁语computare。

搭配:be computed at £5 million:估算为500万英镑

![](images/b3e9fa06e3a309c47fcc09a18e5526a1726270351724b4976da13c7739f265f9.jpg)

compute的派生词或合成词有compute, supercomputer, computer-based, computer-generated, computing, computation, computational, computerized等。

搭配:computing industries:计算机行业

同样表示“计算；数”的词根还有“calc-,-ckon”$^{c}$

搭配: calculate how much/how many etc.: 计算多少(数量)
calculate on an hourly basis: 按小时计算

calculated ['kælkjʊlərtɪd] adj. 蓄意的；精心策划的；处心积虑的〔含贬义〕12821
搭配: be calculated to do sth: 旨在做某事, 用意在于某事

reckon ['rekən] vt. 料想；以为；估算；认为 8695
助记:re-(反复)+\~ckon(=count:认为；计算)→反复认为；计算→认为；估计
搭配:be reckoned as a major quake:被认为是大地震

例句:Melina Kunar of the University of Warwick, and Todd Horowitz of Harvard Medical School ran a series of experiments in which two groups of volunteers had to pay attention and respond to a series of moving tasks on a computer screen that were reckoned equivalent in difficulty to driving.

华威大学的Melina Kunar和哈佛大学医学院的Todd Horowitz做了一些列实验,在试验中两组志愿者要集中精力观察电脑屏幕上的一系列的目标并且做出回应,这被认为与驾驶的困难相同。

![](images/280b4f9c0748d029582f96e9698e572361b221f164f839dcf59a59c7ed5920c3.jpg)

词根“qual-,quan-,quo-”也表示询问数量或程度,一般表示“质量；数量”,隐引申义为“品质；特性；才能”等。

quantity ['kɒwntɪtɪ] n. 数量[+of]; 大量 4100

词源:出现于14世纪早期,来自古法语quantite, cantite(12世纪现代法语quantité),直接来自拉丁语quantitatem(主格为quantitas),表示relative greatness or extent:相对的巨大或程度。来自拉丁语quantus of what size? how much? how great? what amount? 表示什么大小？多少？多大？多少数量？
助记:quant-(量:数量)+-itv(名词后缀)→数量:大量
搭配:huge quantities of oil:大量石油

in quantity:大量；许多

a large/small/vast etc. quantity of sth:很多/很少/大量的某物

in large/small/sufficient etc. quantities: 大量/少量/充足的量

比较:quantity表示数量,quality表示质量；品质。

quality ['kwɒlətɪ] n. 质量；优质；优良品质；个性；特性 765

词源:c. 1300, temperament, character, disposition. 来自古法语qualite=nature, characteristic: 本质; 特性。来自拉丁语qualitatem=a quality, property; nature: 质量; 性质; 本性; 种类。来自qualis=what kind of a: 什么种类; 类型。
助记:qual-(性质；特征；种类)+ -ity(名词后缀)→质量；个性；特征→引申义为优质；优良品质
搭配:a college of quality: 一所优质学院
the quality of life: 生活质量
a childlike quality: 孩子般的个性

quantity 的派生词有 quantify, quantitative, quandary, quantum 等。

quantify [ˈkwɒntɪfɑː] vt.&vi. 确定……的数量；量化 9951
搭配:difficult/impossible to quantify:难以量化/不可能进行量化
quantify the region's economic decline:对该地区经济衰退进行量化

quantitative ['kwpntɪ,tetɪv; -,teɪtɪv] adj. (数)量的；定量的 7803
搭配:quantitative analysis:定量分析
quantitative research:定量研究

quandary ['kwɒnd(ə)rɪ] n. 窘境；进退两难 16185
助记:来自拉丁语quando:何时；什么时候；哪天→表示犹豫,不确定→引申词义困境；进退两难
搭配:in a quandary:左右为难

quantum ['kwɒntəm] n. 量子 adj. 量子的 5768
搭配: quantum mechanics: 量子力学

a quantum leap/quantum jump: (大小、数量的)猛然剧增; (质量的)突飞猛进

quota ['kwəutə] n. 配额；定量[+of] [+for]:(公正的、正确的或正常的)份额[+of]

词源:来自拉丁语quot,多少。用于指战士或士兵的供给定额或配额,后词义通用化。
助记:quot- (=count)+a(一个；一定)→一定的数量→定额；配额
搭配:sales/production quota:销售指标

meet/make/achieve a quota:完成定额

more than its quota of problems:特别多的问题

quality的派生词有qualify, qualifier, qualified, qualification, qualifying, qualitative, qualitatively 等。

qualify ['kwɒlɪfɪ] vt.(通过增加细节、解释)使语气缓和；修饰；限定 vi.取得下一轮比赛资格；取得资格(文凭)vt.&vi. 使……符合(某物的全部特征)；可算作(qualify as)；(使)有资格拥有n. 通过预赛者3075
搭配:to qualify for maternity:有资格休产假
qualify his opinion:补充说明他的观点
qualify sb/sth for sth:使某人有权做……/有资格拥有……

qualifier ['kwɒlɪfɪə(r)] n. 取得参赛资格的人；资格赛；修饰语 16156
搭配:the World Cup qualifier against the Netherlands:对阵荷兰的世界杯预选赛
host the U.S.-Mexico qualifier:举行了美国对墨西哥的预选赛

qualified ['kwɒlɪfɪd] adj. 有资格的；有限度的 6064
搭配:qualified success:局部成功

qualification [ˈkwɒlɪfɪˈkeɪʃ(ə)n] n. 资格；学历；资格取得；技能；限制条件；(已通过的)资格考试 6940
搭配:necessary qualifications:必需的素质
be subject to many qualifications:有许多限制条件

qualifying ['kwɒlɪ,faɪn] adj. 使具有资格的；预赛的 14704
搭配:qualifying performances:排位赛成绩
the qualifying competition:预选赛

qualitative ['kwɒlɪtətɪv] adj. 质量的；定性的；性质的 7214
搭配:a qualitative analysis/study:定性分析/研究

qualitatively [ˈkwɒlə, tetɪvli] adv. 实质上的 18815
搭配:qualitatively different:实质上的差别

"put- to cut, strike, stamp",含义为“削减；切开；撞击；用脚踩踏；跺脚”等。

词源: Proto-Indo-European root meaning "to cut, strike, stamp."

It forms all or part of: account; amputate; amputation; anapest; berate; compute; count (v.); depute; deputy; dispute; impute; pave; pavement; pit (n.1)“hole, cavity;” putative; rate (v.1)“to scold;” reputation; repute.

amputate ['æmpju:tət] vt. 切除；截(肢)17705
助记:am-(=ambi-=around:周围的)+put-(=to cut, prune, trim:切；修剪；切除)+ate(动词后缀)→在周围切除；修剪→原指给树木剪枝,后指医学上人体截肢
搭配:amputate his legs:截去了他的双腿

![](images/e63dcacde9943da84436931e1f169e68b6a65891bd7e8d141154a2a72e1c74b2.jpg)

截肢；切除

amputate 的派生词或合成词有 amputation, amputee 等。

amputation [æmpju'teɪʃn] n. 截肢 13065

amputee [æmpju'tiː] n. 被截肢者 17640

词根“put-”也表示“思考；考虑”

deputy ['depjuti] n. 副职；议员；〔美国〕县行政司法官助理；代理人 2591

词源:c. 1400, "subordinate officer, one given the full power of an officer without holding the office," from Anglo-French député, noun use of past-participle of Old French députer "appoint, assign". 来自盎格鲁-法语deputé。来源于拉丁语putare(计算；考虑)的复合词deputare(分配；指派)。
助记:de- (=away: 离开)+ -put- (=to think, count, consider: 考虑)+ -y (名词后缀)→离开某地(代表……)进行考虑的人→代理人(代表当事人处理事务)；副职(代表正职考虑)；议员(代表某地民众思考如何治理国家)
搭配: the deputy head of a school: 副校长
the Deputy Secretary of State: 助理国务卿

dispute [dɪ'spiju:t; 'dɪspiju:t] n. 争论 vt. 反驳；争夺(控制权、所有权)2726
助记:dis-(=separately, apart: 分离地；与众不同的)+ -put-(=to count, consider: 考虑)+ e→各人想法不一样,各抒己见→引申义争论
搭配:somebody/something in dispute: 人/组织/事物有争议的

dispute the allegations: 驳斥了这些无根据的指控

pay disputes: 工资纠纷

be beyond dispute: 无可争辩,确定无疑

be open to dispute: 可商榷；有争议

undisputed [ʌndr'spjʊ:trd] adj. (事实、观点等)无需争议的；公认的；无异议的(领袖、冠军等)16354
搭配: his undisputed genius: 他那无需争议的天才
the undisputed leader: 公认的领袖

putative ['piju:tətiv] adj. 公认的；推定的 17077
搭配:the putative father of this child:这孩子的推定的父亲

repute [rɪ'piu:t] n. 名声；名望；美名 19741

词源:来自拉丁语reputare “to count over, reckon; think over: 仔细思考；计算；反复考虑。助记:re- (=repeatedly: 反复地)+-put- (=to judge, suppose, believe, suspect: 判断；假定；认为；猜想)+e →反复考虑的→一个人美好的名声引得众人反复思考他/她的品格→引申词义名声；声望；美名
搭配:of repute/of high repute:名声好的；颇有名望的

reputable ['reju:təb(ə)l] adj. 声誉好的；有声望的 14291
搭配:a reputable firm/company:一家声誉好的公司

reputation [repiju'teɪʃ(ə)n] n. 名誉；名望[+ for] [+ as] 2432
搭配:gain a reputation as a hard worker:赢得了勤奋的好口碑

![](images/e3f10435c9928f2864dcb9f4ed0360bbf88127a842e53a2806c1bbc690183f47.jpg)

pave [peɪv] vt. [用石块或混凝土板] 铺 [路、地面等] 7205

词源: early 14c., "to cover (a street)with stones or other material"。14世纪早期, pave就有用石头或其他材料铺街道的含义。来自古法语paver=to pave, 铺路。来自拉丁语pavire=to beat, ram, tread down, 击打, 踩, 践踏。来自词根pau-,砍, 击。
搭配:a paved courtyard:地面铺砌过的院子

pave the way for sth:为……铺平道路；为……创造条件
the streets are paved with gold:遍地是黄金〔表示在某地能迅速发财〕

![](images/e654d160fd9d5e202bb50796d5ef85117cc3847be718ab012d42cc1bba2e996e.jpg)

paving ['peɪvɪŋ] n. 铺路材料 18713
搭配: concrete paving: 混凝土铺路材料

pavement ['peɪvm(ə)nt] n. 路面；人行道 6642
搭配: a pavement café: 路边咖啡馆

hit the pavement: 撞在了路面上

pit [pɪt] n. 矿井；大坑；(赛道旁的)检修加油站；核 vt. 使对立；除去(水果的)核 3894
助记:pit=hole, cavity(洞；凹处)
搭配:pit one's wits against: 与……斗智

in the pit of one's stomach: (因恐惧或焦虑而生的)异于平常的感觉

![](images/6b4a2352f59cb92149ffeb772fc28c1a36dfb3ff735e57ce0c8ba10caa794ec9.jpg)

"rate" 表示 “怒斥”。

词源:古法语reter(指责；归咎),来自(缩写自)拉丁语 reputare,思考,反思→中古英语rate(责骂)→rate(引申词义责骂,怒斥。常见于复合词berate,责备)

berate [br'eit] vt. [+for] 训斥；严厉指责 16426
助记:berate→谐音“必擂他”→必须要擂他一顿→痛骂

be- (=thoroughly: 彻底地)+rate (=to scold: 责骂)→严厉斥责
搭配:berate Joe for the noise he made: 指责乔制造的噪声

![](images/503623ba283b17c0f049c68eb9b9d343b4809d9934944dce027aca3c205ab713.jpg)

a calculated attempt to seduce Snow White to eat the poison apple
白雪公主的后母处心积虑诱惑她吃毒苹果

"qu-" 开头的单词一般表示 "who, which, how, why, where, in what respect, to what extent", 即英文中的特殊疑问词, 如 "what, when, whence, where, whether, which, whither, who, whoever, whom, whose, why, how" 等单词都是源于 "qu-" 这个词根。

"query" 表示 "提问","quest" 表示 "探求；寻求"

query ['kwiərɪ] n. 疏问 vt. 对……提出疑问；询问 10092

词源:1530s, quaere “a question,” from Latin quaere “ask,” imperative of quaere “to seek, look for; strive, endeavor, strive to gain; ask, require, demand;” figuratively “seek mentally, seek to learn, make inquiry”. 来自拉丁语quaere=a question, ask: 疏问；询问；查问
搭配:query your bill:对账单提出质疑
have any queries:有任何疑问

quest [kwest] n. (长久而艰难的)搜寻; 探求 vi. 搜寻; 探求 4108

词源: c. 1300, "an inquest;" early 14c., "a search for something" (especially of judicial inquiries or hounds seeking game), from Old French queste "search, quest, chase, hunt, pursuit; inquest, inquiry" (12c., Modern French quête), properly "the act of seeking," and directly from Medieval Latin questa "search, inquiry," alteration of Latin quaesitus (fem. quaesita)"sought-out, select," past participle of quaere "seek, gain, ask".
助记:quest(=seek:寻求；搜索)→寻求；搜寻
搭配:in quest of something:寻找某物

the quest for a better bank:搜寻一家更好的银行

his questing mind and boundless enthusiasm: 他的探索型头脑和无限的热情

例句:Job-hunting tasks gain added meaning as you sense their importance in your quest for a more meaningful work life.

找工作能获得更多的意义,因为你在寻求一个更有意义的工作生活时意识到了他们的重要性。

quest的派生词有request, question, unquestioned, questionable, unquestionably, questioner, questioning, questionnaire 等。

request [rɪ'kwest] vt. 请求；正式要求 n. 请求 2134
助记:re-(=repeatedly:反复地)+quest(探求)→反复地探求→请求；正式要求
搭配:at someone's request:应某人的要求

on request:应要求

at the request of: 应……的邀请, 应……的要求

request for: 要求

question ['kwestʃ(ə)n] n. 问题；询问；疑问；(需考虑的)问题；试题 vt. 询问；怀疑 197
搭配:in question:正被提及的；有关的
out of the question:完全不可能的
pop the question:求婚

there is no question of: ……是不可能的

unquestioned [ʌn'kwestʃ(ə)nd] adj. 无可置疑的；无可争议的；不加质询的
19163
搭配: the unquestioned ruler of: ……无可争议的领导者
give unquestioned obedience to authority: 对权威不加质询地顺从

questionable ['kwestʃ(ə)nəb(ə)l] adj. 可疑的；不合理的 6337
搭配:questionable business practices: 可疑的商业行为

unquestionably [ʌn'kwəstʃənbli] adv. 毫无疑问地, 无可置疑地, 肯定地

13696

questioner ['kwestʃənə] n. 提问者 18594

cue [kju:] n. (戏剧中暗示下一位演员接言或出场的)尾白, 提示; 提示; 暗示[+for]; 触发事件 vt. (尤指在表演中)提示 4929

词源: 在16和17世纪时, 在西方戏剧的脚本上, 往往有表示提醒演员说话或上场的提示符号Q, Q是拉丁单词quando (=英语中的when)的缩写。后来, 这个符号逐渐演变为单词cue, 其发音跟Q一样。词义也逐渐扩展, 不仅可以用来表示戏剧中的提示, 还可以表示任何 “提示”, 泛指 “暗示”。
搭配:(right/as if)on cue:恰好；正好
cue ball:撞球台上的白色球；母球

词根 -quire 可以表示 “获得”,是与单词 “hold: 获得,拥有” 同源,词根 “-quer, -quis” 均表示 “获得,得到”

acquire [ə'kwaɪə] vt. 购得；获得；学到(知识、技能)2079
助记:ac- (=ad-:去；表强调)+ -quir- (=to seek to obtain: 寻求获得)+ e→gain, earn, procure: 获得；得到；赚得；购买→购得；获得；学到
搭配:acquire an email address: 获得了一个电子邮件地址

acquire a reputation for...: 以……而闻名

acquire a good knowledge of Chinese: 汉语学得很好

例句:A patient may also acquire a tolerance for a certain drug, which means the patient has to take ever larger doses to produce the desired effect.

病人对于某种药可能获得了一种抗药性,这就意味着病人不得不服用更大剂量的要去达到想要的效果。

![](images/10cb99da0c26a410d49012ac3a0bbde3685f0699d6db37416b1d2dd4501d4d74.jpg)

acquire 的派生词有 acquired, acquisition 等。

acquired [ə'kwaɪd] adj. 后天获得(习得)的 15638
搭配:acquired right:既得权益 acquired taste:嗜好；爱好

AIDS [edz] abbr. 获得性免疫缺乏综合症；爱滋病(Acquired Immune Deficiency Syndrome)2021

acquisition [ˌækwɪˈzɪʃ(ə)n] n. 收购；获得；习得 3893
搭配:the acquisition of a company:收购一家公司
make this marvelous acquisition:进行这宗不可思议的购置
language acquisition:语言习得

conquer ['kɒŋkə] vt. 征服；攻占；克服 6840
助记:con-(=com-；表加强)+ -quer(=to gain:获得；得到)→获得(别人的)土地；得到(他国)的国土→征服；攻占；克服
搭配:conquer our differences:消除我们的分歧
conquer his addiction to smoking:戒除过烟瘾
divide and conquer:分而治之；各个击破

![](images/18fc123c2b117b794766fc2488b14abccfd73b5585aeaaa958e95f06bc816e37.jpg)

conquer 的派生词有 conquering, conqueror, conquest 等。

搭配:worth conquering:值得征服
succeed in conquering the difficult mountain:成功地征服了那座难以攀登的山

搭配:William the Conqueror:征服者威廉(英格兰国王威廉一世)
obey their conquerors:顺从他们的征服者

conquest ['kɒŋkwest] n. 征服；克服 7790
搭配:the Spanish conquest of Mexico:西班牙人对墨西哥的征服

![](images/ccb3500f82ed4b0b19450e855d4ed7e4aae0424a38b2cd781d09be8c0e406628.jpg)

词根“-quire”除了表示“获得,得到”外,还可以表示“寻求,要求”,此时与单词“seek:寻求,要求(=ask)”同源。

inquire [ɪn'kwaɪə] vt.&vi. 查询；打听 vi. 调查；查究 6787
助记:in-(进入；使)+quir(问询；寻求)+e→查询；调查
搭配:inquire about job possibilities:打听就业的可能性

inquire into the affairs of the company:调查该公司的事务

![](images/eca655d13572c34e5352644135c850fa2d9930e9831205f7953801b1647326e4.jpg)

inquire 的派生词有 inquiry, inquisitive 等。

inquiry [ɪn'kwaɪrɪ] n. 询问；(官方的)调查；调查 3396
助记:in-(内部)+ -quir (=seek:寻求；探寻)+y(名词后缀)→向内寻找；寻求→询问；探究；调查
搭配:make some inquiries:询问一番
a shocking murder inquiry:一例令人震惊的谋杀案调查
a new line of inquiry:一种新的探询方法

inquisitive [ɪn'kwɪzɪtɪv] adj. 好奇的；爱打听的 17841
搭配: have an inquisitive nature: 生性好奇

require [rɪ'kwaɪə] vt. 需要；要求 447
助记:re-(=repeatedly:反复地)+-quire(=ask, seek: 要求；寻求)→反复
寻求；反复要求→需求；要求
搭配:require sb to do sth:要求某人做某事

![](images/25c974dbe89900898b91cb20ba1fe6b88e93c421b89e967ff2bca6b6b1f68e96.jpg)

require 的派生词有 required, requisite, requirement 等。

required [rɪ'kwaɪd] adj. 必需的；(美)必修的 4507
搭配:required course:必修课程

requisite [ˈrekwɪzɪt] adj. 必要的 n. 必需品 12513
搭配:the requisite paperwork:必需的文件
a requisite for the work of the analysts:对于分析师的工作是必需的

requirement [rɪ'kwaɪmənt] n. 必要条件需要；必需品 1899
搭配:meet/satisfy/fulfill one's requirements/needs/demands:满足某人的要求/需要
助记:pre-(=before:在前)+requi(=require:要求)+s + -ite(名词后缀)→something required beforehand:事前、提前提出的要求→先

决条件
助记:缩写自perquisite,津贴,额外补贴。per-(完全的)+quis(要求；探索)+ite(名词后缀)→完全、彻底的要求→引申词义过分要求,特权→后来也用于指额外收入,津贴拿到额外收入,津贴会让人精神振奋→使活跃；振作起来
搭配: theatre tickets and other perks: 戏票以及其他补贴

the perks of working at a large law firm: 在大型律师事务所工作的额外待遇

perk sb up: 昂首翘尾; 活跃起来; 振作精神

perk up the sauce: 使酱汁更有味

perky ['pɜːkɪ] adj. 自信而愉快的；活泼的,生气勃勃的 19407

词源:来自古英语perquer,栖息,休息,词源同perch。原指鸟栖息或整理羽毛,引申词义休息好的,兴奋的,有精力的。
助记:perk(使活跃,振作起来)+-y(形容词后缀)→活泼的,生气勃勃的→自信而愉快的
搭配:a perky sales girl:精力充沛的女店员

perch [pɜːtʃ] vi. 轻坐在；坐落于；(鸟)栖息 vt. 把……稳置于(某物顶部或边缘)n. (鸟的)栖木 6165
助记:“where a bird rests,” late 13c., originally only “a pole, rod, stick, stake,” from Old French perche “unit of linear measurement” (5.5 yards), also “measuring rod, pole, bar” used to measure this length (13c.), from Latin pertica “pole, long staff, measuring rod.” 后用于指鸟栖息的横杆,引申词义栖息,停留。
搭配:sit on its perch:站在栖木上
perch on top of the hills:坐落于群山之顶端

词根“ject-”表示“喷；扔；投；射”。

![](images/630f39b6c16e72971f72eaf38940647bb450e7102515840ebbd862fd5f7710bc.jpg)

如何记住 “jet” 表示 “喷, 扔; 投; 射”, 可由短语 jet plane: 喷气式飞机来记忆

![](images/18d460a85349456e27873cd11882fd1e8869f589ee9e35debb960a4c8019825f.jpg)

词源:*yē-,Proto-Indo-European root meaning "to throw, impel."

It is the hypothetical source of/evidence for its existence is provided by: Hittite ijami "I make;" Greek iemi, ienai "to send, throw;" Latin iacere "to throw, cast."

project [prə'dʒekt; 'prɒdʒekt] n. 项目；课题[+on] vt. 预计；投射 vi. 凸出；突出[+out/from/through etc] 535
助记:pro-(向前)+ject(=jet:投；喷；射；c发k音无意义)→向前投；掷→投影；项目(实施前都要“向前投递”给上司过目)
搭配:be projected to do sth:预计做某事

project [+out/from/through etc.]: 从……上面凸出

(阅读,写作)例句:

By accepting who you are – all your emotions, hopes and dreams, your personality, and your unique way of being – you'll project more confidence when networking and talking with potential employers.

通过接受你自己——你所有的情感、希望和梦想、你的个性、以及你

存在的独特性——当你在和潜在的雇主交流和谈话时,你将会投射出更多的自信。

![](images/f8a32899e2b09e98c7ff4d3e34c5a7c603346c5c877ca18c2da76c0492856e41.jpg)

与 project 同样表达凸出含义的词汇还有 jut。

jut [dʒʌt] vi. 突出；伸出[后面总跟+adv/prep] vt. 将〔下巴〕翘起 11433
助记:来自拉丁语iacere,投,扔,词源同project,projectile。即向前扔出去,引申词义突出,伸出。
搭配:jut out over the beach: 突兀于海滩之上

jut her chin out: 抬起她的下巴

![](images/1b739b9c66437266613ef59af3eabcabff27e0cfaba0cf5a8aba125a5339efec.jpg)

project 的派生词有 projected, projectile, projecting, projection, projector 等。

projected [prə'dʒektɪd] adj. 投影的；预计的 7047
搭配:projected area:投影面积
projected workload:预定工作量

projectile [prə(u)'dʒektail; -tɪl] n. 投掷物；发射物〔如子弹、石头或炮弹〕 16467
助记:rocket projectile:火箭弹

projecting [prəu'dzektɪn] adj. 突出的；投影的 17356
搭配:projecting camera:投影机
projecting structure:伸出楼外的构筑物

projection [prə'dʒekʃ(ə)n] n. 预计[+of] [+for]; 凸出物; (幻灯片、电影的)投映 4809
搭配:projections of declining natural gas production:对呈下降趋势的天然气产量的预测

small projections of weathered rock on the hillside:山坡上许多凸出的小块风化岩石

projection equipment:投影设备

projector [prə'dʒektə] n. 电影放映机；投影仪 10560
搭配:a slide projector:幻灯机

inject [ɪn'dʒekt] vt. 给……注射；注入；增添；注入(资金或资源)5672
助记:in-(里面)+ject(投；射)→向里面射→注射
搭配:inject strong drugs:注射了强效的药

inject $750 into the banks:向银行投入750美元

例句:Anthony Atala, director of the Wake Forest Institute in North Carolina, believes failing organs will be repaired by injecting cells into the body.

北卡罗来纳州维克森林学院的院长Anthony Atala认为,可以通过向体内注射细胞的方法来修复受损的器官。

![](images/46c8dc61996b3c894f38bec68b3a62f7a4a53a9c451f47799c5e8e376765ec3a.jpg)

injection [ɪn'dʒekʃ(ə)n] n. 注射；(资金或资源的)注入 5812
搭配:drug injection:药物注射
an injection of cash:投入现金

object ['bɒdʒɪkt; -dʒekt] n. 物体；目的；(某情感或反应的)对象；宾语 vt. 反对 1156

UFO [,ju:ef'əʊ] abbr. 不明飞行物(Unidentified Flying Object)12613
助记:ob-(=against:反对)+ject(=to throw:扔；投)→朝反面扔→反对；拒绝接受
搭配:money is no object/distance is no object:金钱/距离不是问题
object to sth:反对某事

![](images/323b7ed3575c7821e20ede23f4646c02a7205986b0f484eada1d683b4cbbfee3.jpg)

object的派生词有objection, objectionable, objective, objectively, objectivity 等。

objection [əb'dʒekʃ(ə)n] n. 反对[+to]; 异议 4789
搭配:over the objections of sb (=in spite of their objections):尽管某人反对

objectionable [əb'dʒekʃ(ə)nəb(ə)l] adj. 令人反感的；令人不能接受的 15740
搭配: objectionable odours: 难闻的气味

objective [əb'dʒektɪv] adj. (尤指商业或政治方面的)目标；(尤指军事行动中的)攻击目标 adj. 客观的；真实的 2427
搭配:purely/totally/competpletely objective: 完全客观的

core objectives: 核心目标

objectively [əb'dʒektɪvli] adv. 客观地 12825
搭配:look at the skills objectively:客观地考虑技能

objectivity [ˌɒbdʒekˈtrɪvɪtɪ; ˌɒbdʒɪkˈtrɪvɪtɪ] n. 客观 10722
搭配:with poise and objectivity:带着镇定和客观

比较: object: 物体; 客体→objective [əb'dʒektɪv] adj. 客观的 n. 目标

subject: 主体; 主题→subjective [səb'dʒektɪv] adj. 主观的; 个人的

subject ['sʌbdʒɪkt; (for adj.); sʌbdʒɪkt; (for v.)səb'dʒekt] n. 主题；对象；科目；实验对象；(绘画、摄影等的)题材；主语；(常指君主制国家的)臣民 adj. 受……影响的；受……支配的 vt. 使遭受 670
助记:sub-(次)+ject(扔；放)→扔在次要位置→引申词义被制服；被控制→从属于(主要)；臣民

sub-(下)+ject(扔)→扔在……之下→常遭受…(比如:将某地区“扔”到暴风雪之下,即:该地区“经常遭受”暴风雪)

sub-(下)+ject(扔)→被扔到(某实验/研究之)下→(成了实验的)对象:主题:科目:题材
搭配:be subject to:从属于……；受制于；以……为准；经受……

change the subject: 转变话题

例句:In contrast, our image of the astronomical universe, of even of earth's geological history, can easily be subject to revolutionary changes as new data comes in and new theories are worked out.

相比之下,我们对天文学领域的映像,甚至是对地球地质的历史都会随着新数据和新理论的出现而遭受殖民性变化。

写作例句:很多正版产品都遭受到盗版的冲击,这导致从事原创性工作的人越来越少。

Many genuine products are subject to the impact of pirated products, which leads to a sharp decrease in the people who are engaged in original work.

![](images/d530d5485915e55c7a05dab42fb43d156d839b38d898ea5f8997992d85540cbf.jpg)

subject 的派生词有 subjective, subjectivity 等。

subjective [səb'dʒektɪv] adj. 主观的；主观想象的；主语的 6033
搭配:subjective judgment/opinion etc.: 主管判断/意见

subjectivity [,sʌbdʒek'tɪvəti] n. 主观性 11947
搭配:the subjectivity of clothing designers:设计师的主观性

reject [(for v.)rɪ'dʒekt; 'ri:dʒekt] vt. 拒绝接受[相信或赞同]；拒绝(录用或录取)；拒绝(某人的爱情)；排斥(移植的器官等)；〔因质量不好而〕废弃 n. 次品；被排斥者 2046
助记:re-(回)+ject(扔)→扔回来→拒绝；抛弃(比如:送花示爱被扔回来)
搭配:reject the idea:拒绝了这个想法

shop selling cheap rejects: 销售廉价次品的商店

rejection [rɪ'dʒekʃ(ə)n] n. 拒绝接受[相信；赞同]；否决[+of]；(对求职者、求学者等的)拒绝；嫌弃 5063
搭配: his rejection of the theory: 他不接受这个理论

a rejection letter: 一封回绝信

a feeling of rejection and loss: 一种遭人嫌弃的失落感

仿写例句:鼓励大学生们拒绝去过有挑战的生活让它们在困难和挫折前感到脆弱不堪。

Inspiring/Encouraging college students to reject/maintain rejection to the life full of challenges makes them fragile to exploitation and control.

trajectory [trə'dʒekt(ə)rɪ; 'trædʒɪkt(ə)rɪ] n. 抛物线；(物体射向或抛向空中形成的)轨迹；(事物的)发展轨迹 7885
助记:tra-(=trans:横过；越过)+ -ject-(=to throw:投；射)+ -ory(名词后缀)→物体横过上空投射形成的曲线或轨迹→引申词义抛物线；轨迹:弹道；发展轨迹等

abject ['æbdʒekt] adj. 糟糕透顶的；自卑的 17227
助记:ab- (=off, away from: 分离)+ -ject (=to throw: 投; 射)→即扔掉的→引申词义downcast, brought low, hopeless: 悲惨的; 自卑的
搭配: abject poverty/misery/failure etc.: 赤贫/凄苦/惨败等

an abject apology: 低声下气的道歉

adjacent [ə'dʒeɪs(ə)nt] adj. 邻近的；毗连的[+to] 6752
助记:ad-(=to:去)+jac-(=to lie, rest: 躺下；休息；依靠)+-ent(形容词后缀)→lie at, border upon, lie near→躺在旁边的→contiguous, bordering, close, nearby:相邻的；毗连的

趣味记忆:谐音“爱得贼深的”→爱得深,所以难舍难分
搭配:adjacent sea:近海

the building adjacent to the library:紧挨着图书馆的建筑

词源:“word used to qualify, limit, or define a noun or noun-like part of speech,” late 14c., short for noun adjective, from Old French adjectif (14c.), from Latin adjectivum “that is added to (the noun),” neuter of adjectivus “added”.
助记: ad- (=to: 来; 临近)+ -ject- (=to throw: 投; 射)+ -ive(形容词后缀)→throw to, fling at, throw or place (a thing)near: 扔到主语附近, 附加以修饰名词的→形容词
搭配: adjective clause: 形容词从句

conjecture [kən'dʒektʃə] n. 推测；猜测 vt.&vi. 推测；猜测 15060
助记:con- (=together: 共同)+ -ject- (=to throw: 投; 射)+ -ure (名词后缀)→共同投射思想→猜测；推测
搭配:several conjectures: 几种推测

pure conjecture: 纯属猜测

Goldbach conjecture: 哥德巴赫猜想(任何比2大的偶数都是两质数的和)

eject [i'dʒekt] vt. 逐出；用力推出 vi. (从飞机里)弹射出来 11221
助记: e- (=out: 出来)+ -ject (=to throw: 扔; 投; 射)→ 扔出来 → 逐出;

用力推出; 弹射出来
搭配: eject from the plane: 从飞机里弹出
助记:inter-(=between:在中间)+ject(=to throw:投；扔)→to throw between, set between→在中间插入→插嘴

jet [dʒet] n. 喷气式飞机；喷射流；黑玉 vi. 乘喷气式飞机前往；喷出 3170

词源:来自中古法语jeter, 抛, 投掷。来自拉丁语jactare。来自jacere: 抛; 投掷→引申词义水流; 喷水嘴; 喷气; 喷气式飞机等。词源同eject, project, 字母c脱落。
助记: jet=ject→to throw: 投; 射→喷气; 射水; 喷气式飞机; 喷射流; 喷出
搭配: a jet of water: 一股水柱

jet off to Germany: 乘喷气式飞机去德国

jet earrings: 黑玉耳环

![](images/705e2c57c5f30dcc3cd7d506a3e4d8ed71a0bc35cf53ab7fdc28c86151952fe8.jpg)

jet 的派生词有 jetliner 等。

.jetliner ['dʒetlaɪnə] n. 大型(客运)喷气机 19859

jettison ['dʒetɪs(ə)n; -z(ə)n] vt. 拒绝接受；丢弃；处理掉 16717

jetty ['dʒetɪ] n. 码头；防波堤 adj. 黑玉的；(颜色和光泽)像黑玉的 19732

![](images/560f2b71b1eedcee1258e05e82297ce4bb119ad15733e98438d7a9b1c1ce60fc.jpg)

以 iect- 为词根的单词还有 ease, gist, joist, iut 等。

ease [i:z] n. 简便；舒适 vt.&vi. 减轻；小心慢慢地移动 3257
搭配:with ease:轻易地
at ease:自在的
ill at ease:不自在的

gist [dʒɪst] n. 要点 18471

joist [dɔːɪst] n. 棺栅；托梁 19892

词根“fuse=pour”,含义为“融合；浇铸；倾倒”,名词含义为“爆炸物的引信”。

词源:*gheu

Proto-Indo-European root meaning "to pour, pour a libation."

It is the hypothetical source of/evidence for its existence is provided by: Greek khein "to pour," khoane "funnel," khymos "juice;" Latin fundere (past participle fusus)"melt, cast, pour out;" Gothic giutan, Old English geotan "to pour;" Old English guttas (plural)"bowels, entrails;" Old Norse geysa "to gush;" German Gosse "gutter, drain."

fuse [fju:z] n. 保险丝；导火线 vt.&vi. (物理地/特质/思想等)结合；融合；使〔保险丝〕熔断 10616

词源:来自拉丁语fundere=melt, cast, pour out: 熔化；浇铸；倾注。词源同foundry, alchemy, confused. 用于冶炼学术语,如冶金；炼铁；玻璃冶炼等→引申词义融化；融合
搭配:blow a fuse:烧断保险丝

a short fuse: 人的火爆脾气

fuse (sth)with sth: 将……与……结合

fuse (sth)into: 将……合并入

fuse的派生词有fuselage, fusion, defuse, confuse, refuse, diffuse, infuse, profuse, suffuse 等。

fuselage ['fju:zəla:z; -lɪdʒ] (飞机、火箭的)机身；(导弹的)弹身 17033
搭配: rip apart the plane's fuselage: 使该飞机的机身断裂

fusion ['fju:ʒ(ə)n] n. 融合；熔合；融为一体；核聚变 7363
搭配:the fusions of jazz, pop and African melodies have proved highly successful: 爵士乐、流行乐和非洲音乐旋律的融合

the fusion of regular and reserve forces: 把常规军和后备军合二为一

research into nuclear fusion: 对核聚变的研究

defuse [di:'fju:z] vt. 缓和；拆除……的引言 12812
助记:de-(=undo-:除去；破坏)+fuse(引信)→即拆除引信→引申义缓和
搭配:defuse potentially violent situations:缓和潜在的暴力情势
defuse a bomb:拆除一枚炸弹

confuse [kən'fju:z] vt. 混淆；使困惑；使复杂化 n. 混淆 3550
助记:con-(全部)+-fuse(=pour:倾倒；流)→(把各种液体)倒到一起→混；混乱
搭配:be/get/become confused with sth:对……感到困惑
confuse the issue/matter/argument etc.:使问题/事情/争论等更加复杂

![](images/cb810570bcb25da045220cef800f240c1806789b17107ee9ba6d2ce094d83e1b.jpg)

confuse 的派生词有 confused, confusing, confusion 等。

confused [kən'fju:zd] adj. 困惑的[+about]; 混乱的 5718
搭配:a lot of confused ideas:许多混淆的观念

辨析:confused〔因不理解而〕困惑的；糊涂的
puzzled〔尤因事情和预料的不同而〕困惑的；迷惑的
baffled(因尝试很久也没有解决而)非常困惑的

confusing [kən'fju:zɪŋ] adj. 令人困惑的；难懂的 6319
搭配:a very confusing situation:非常混乱的局面

confusion [kən'fju:ʒ(ə)n] n. 混乱[+ about/over/as to]; 混淆[+between]; 寨迫 3362
搭配:create/lead to confusion:造成混乱
in confusion:不知所措地

refuse [rɪ'fjuːz] n. 垃圾；废料 vt.&vi. 拒绝 vt. 拒绝给予；拒绝 1253
助记:re-(=back:回)+fuse(=to pour:流)→(东西被)流回来→(被)拒绝
搭配:refuse him a visa:拒绝给予他签证
refuse landfill:垃圾填埋

refusal [rɪ'fjuːz(ə)l] n. 拒绝[+to do/of] 6018
搭配:first refusal:优先购买权

diffuse [dr'fju:z] vt.&vi. 传播(知识、信息等)；扩散[+through/into/across]
vt. 缓解(不良情绪或局面)；使(光线)漫射 vi. 扩散 n. (对知识、
消息等的)传播；散布；扩散 adj. 散开的；累赘的 12763
助记:dis-(=apart, in every direction: 分开地；各个方向)+fuse(=to pour: 流)→分开流；即(光线、信息、情绪等)向不同方向流出,漫射开→扩散；传播；缓解；漫射
搭配: diffuse into the soil: 渗进了土壤
diffuse quickly across Europe: 很快在欧洲传播开来
an attempt to diffuse his anger: 平息他怒气的尝试

例句:Alvarez's experience demonstrates the importance of finding ways to diffuse stress before it threatens$^{17}$ your health and your ability to function.
阿尔瓦雷兹的经历说明了在压力影响到你的健康和活动能力之前寻求途径予以排解是相当重要的。

仿写例句:在压力影响到你的健康和活动能力之前寻求途径予以排解是相当重要的。

Finding ways to diffuse/relieve stress before it threatens your health and your ability to function is important.

![](images/8750799b79da454ee379393f1647080bc1a416df84f47cd436f5bf7794546135.jpg)

diffusion [drɪ'fjuːz(ə)n] n. 扩散；传播；[物]漫射 11375

infuse [ɪn'fjuːz] vt. 使充满〔某种感觉〕；向……灌输〔某一品质〕 vt.&vi.〔用热水〕泡(茶或香草)9060
搭配:infuse fresh interest into:把有创意的元素带入

![](images/f82508c55696ef1339d7c4284e4ec502d00374a630a9ee99898ccffc593d595e.jpg)

infuse 的派生词有 infusion 等。

infusion [ɪn'fjuːz(ə)n] n. (新感觉或品质的)注入[+of]; [医]注射；注射用药物；草药泡剂；用香草泡的茶 10321
搭配:the infusion of more resources:要更多资源的注入

profuse [prə'fju:s] adj. 大量(产生)的；丰富的；充沛的；多次的(感谢或道歉)

词源: early 15c., "lavish, extravagant," from Latin profusus "spread out, lavish, extravagant," literally "poured forth," noun use of past participle of profundere "pour forth". Meaning "bountiful" is from c. 1600. Related: Profusely; profuseness.
助记:pro-(=forward:向前)+fuse(=to pour:倾倒)→pour forth:向前倾倒→涌出；流出→引申词义丰富的；大量的

![](images/f9740fed82b8c22a092e4d5dbe20230ebd13fb544f5eae923f42d68e89c662fb.jpg)

profuse 的派生词有 profusely, profusion 等。

搭配:bleed profusely:大量出血
apologize profusely:连连道歉

profusion [prə'fɪʊʒ(ə)n] n. 大量；丰富；充沛[+ of] 16593
搭配:a profusion of wild flowers along its banks:岸上开满了野花

suffuse [sə'fjuːz] vt. (温暖、颜色、液体等)遍布；充满 17821
搭配:be suffused with sth:充满某种情感
be suffused with happiness:心中充满喜悦

![](images/fd3d96676269a6cf446be5b5a3f27a33b31cb26b129a11714303085a3f8d8815.jpg)

以 gheu- 为词根,表示流出的单词还有 geyser, gush, gust, gut, gutsy 等。

geyser ['gi:zə; 'gai-] n. 间歇泉；(厨房或浴室/建筑物的)煤气热水器；电热水器；热水锅炉 17325
助记:来自词根gheu-,含义为喷涌→引申义为间歇泉；热水器；热水锅炉

gush [gʌʃ] vt.&vi. 涌出；夸张地赞扬 n. 涌流 11549
助记:a gush of water:一股流水涌出

a gushing speech:一场阿谀的演说

gust [gʌst] n. 一阵强风；(感情的)迸发 vi. 劲吹 10382
助记:a gust of wind:一阵狂风
a small gust of pleasure:一丝愉悦的迸发

gut [gʌt] n. 内脏；肠；胆量；肚脐；(用于制网球拍、琴弦等的)肠线
adj. 直觉的 vt. 损毁(建筑物)的内部 4340
助记:working sb's guts out:拼命工作
hate someone's guts:对某人恨之入骨
a gut feeling/reaction:本能的感觉/反应
the guts of the problem:问题的实质

gutsy ['gʌtsɪ] adj. 勇敢的；坚定的 19374
助记:gutsy and emotional speech:坚定而饱含深情的讲话
a gutsy performance:一次无畏之举
a gutsy full-bodied wine:烈性、浓郁的葡萄酒

funnel ['fʌn(ə)l] n. 漏斗；〔蒸汽机或轮船的〕烟囱；漏斗状物 vt.&vi. 使经过狭窄空间 vt. 传送(资金、商品、信息等)11059

词源:shortened from Latin infundibulum "a funnel or hopper in a mill," from infundere "pour in," from in- "in" + fundere "to pour。缩写自拉丁语 infundibulum, 工厂灰斗或漏斗。in-(使；进入)+fund(注入)+bulum(工具格后缀)→使……注入的工具→漏斗后也用于指烟囱。
搭配:funnels of dark grey smoke:成漏斗状的暗灰色烟
funnel down the valley:穿过山谷

![](images/f498b7572638506eb0da02a8c154f258b33f5e3f85ff0c477c1a345152cccea4.jpg)

漏斗状物

found [faund] vt. (将金属或玻璃熔化后倒进模型里)浇铸 2687

词源:来自拉丁语fundere(倾注；倾泻),词源同gefser, fusion, alchemy, confound→引申义为(将金属或玻璃熔化后倒进模型里)浇铸,用于冶金学
助记:con-(=together:强调)+found(=to pour:流；倾泻)→即流到一起的；难以区别而困惑的→引申义为挫败(敌人、计划等)；(问题等)把……难住:使不知所措

dumbfound [dʌm'faʊnd] vt. 使惊呆；使人惊愕失声 19877
助记:dumb(哑的；无声音的)+found(=confound的尾词found:使吃惊)→strike dumb with confusion or perplexity:因困惑而吃惊地说不出话来→使惊呆；使人惊愕失声

foundry ['faʊndri] n. 铸造(金属或玻璃的)工厂 18943

font [fɒnt] n. 字体 14241
助记:from Middle French fonte "a casting",含义为铸造。来自拉丁语词根fund=to melt, cast, pour out: 融化；浇铸；倒出。词源同foundry。用于古代的印刷技术,同一版面通常字体一样,因此,该词也用来指字体。

alchemy ['ælkɪmɪ] n. 炼金术；魔法 17780

词源:来源于阿拉伯语alkimya(炼金术),其中al-在阿拉伯语中是定冠词,相当于英语中的the,-kimya来源于希腊语khemia(炼金术)。同词根fund=to pour out,含义为注入。西方16世纪前,化学领域研究的主要方向就是尝试用不同的方法把普通金属冶炼成金子,后随着化学的发展衍生出chemistry专指“化学”。

futile [ˈfɪtəʊtaɪl] adj. 无用的；徒劳的 9583

词源:来自拉丁语fundere(倾注；倾泻)的派生词futilis(渗漏的；徒劳的)→流走的,漏掉的→徒劳的
搭配:a futile attempt/effort:徒劳之举
it is futile to do sth:……是枉然

futility [fju'tɪlɪtɪ; fjuː'tɪlɪtɪ] n. 无谓；徒劳 13938
搭配:thoughts on the futility of war:战争无益思想

词根 “ju-, jur-, jure-, jury-, just” 有 “公平；正义；审判；司法；法律” 等含义。来源于拉丁语词根 -ius 含义为 a right, 一项权利。特别指 legal right or authority, law, 法律权利或权威, 法律。同时, 也指司法的地方, 法院。

just [dʒʌst] adj. 正义的 adv. 刚刚；正要；正(表强调)；只不过；只是；仅仅；只会(造成不良后果)；勉强地；也许；就是(加强表示感情的语气)；简直(表示能想象出)66

词源: 在古希腊神话里, 主持正义和秩序的女神是忒弥斯 (Themis), 是天神乌拉诺斯和大地女神盖亚所生, 十二泰坦神之一, 宙斯的第二任妻子。在古罗马神话中, 正义女神的名字叫做 “朱斯提提亚” (Justitia)。正义女神朱斯提提亚的塑像经常出现在法院中。她的形象通常是身披白袍, 双眼蒙布, 左手提一秤, 右手举一剑。白袍象征道德无瑕, 刚直不阿; 蒙眼代表理性判断, 不受感官和人情影响; 秤象征公平; 剑表示严厉制裁。造像的背面往往刻有古罗马的法谚: “为实现正义, 哪怕天崩地裂。”从朱斯提提亚的名字Justitia中产生了词根just、jur-(法律；正义)、just(公正的)等诸多与法律相关的词汇。

词源:来自拉丁语iustus:公正的；正直的。来自-ius:法律；权利；正义。来自古拉丁语ious:神圣的语言。来自词根yewes-:法规；法则。词源同judge；jury。该词原为古代宗教仪式术语,宗教仪式有着固定的程序和规则,以及繁琐的礼节并向天、地、神起誓的固定用语,因此,引申出法律,发誓这两个主要词义。
助记:单词just可以表示“公正的”是与单词“judge:法官；审判”同源(审判要求“公平:公正”)
搭配:fight a just war:打一场正义的战争

just bought a new house:刚买了一个新房子

iust then:正在那时

just a suggestion:只是一个建议

just a minute/just a moment: 稍等

just a second/just a moment: 等一下, 表插话用

just see or hear something: 简直(表示能想像出)

just like, just as...as, and just the same: 同……一样
just about the best golfer in the world: 算是世界上最优秀的高尔夫球手
just about tolerate it: 勉强可以接受它

![](images/c507fd5c967f86febd0d04c08a8b7d0e5448549012f65401dbc666449b473227.jpg)

just的派生词有unjust, justly, justice, injustice, justify, justified, justification, justifiable, justifiably 等。

unjust [ʌn'dʒʌst] adj. 不公正的 11143
搭配:unjust laws:不公正的法律

justly ['dʒʌs(t)lɪ] adv. 理所应当地；正义的 17739
搭配: be justly proud of their native wildlife: 理应为他们本土的野生动植物而自豪

be treated justly: 被公正地对待

justice ['dʒʌstɪs] n. 司法制度；法律制裁；公正；正义 1490
助记:just-(公平的；正义的)+-ice(名词后缀)→公正；正义；司法制度；法律制裁
搭配:the Justice Department:司法部门
criminal justice system:刑事司法体系
搭配: the injustice of slavery: 奴隶制的不公正

do sb an injustice: 冤枉某人

innumerable injustices against the black population: 对黑人难以计数的不公正行为

justify ['dʒʌstɪfɪ] vi. 证明……有道理；为……辩护；是……的正当理由；使排齐 2857
助记:just(公平的；正义的)+ify(使动词)→使……公平→证明……有道理；为……辩护；是……的正当理由
搭配:justify doing sth:解释做……是正当的

justify yourself (=prove that what you are doing is reasonable): 为自己辩解
justify text: 使文本排齐

释义:(VERB)证明(决定、行为或想法)正当；表明……必要

To justify a decision, action, or idea means to show or prove that it is reasonable or necessary.

(VERB)调整(打印文本):使齐行:使每行排齐

To justify printed text means to adjust the spaces between the words so that each line of type is exactly the same length.

例句:As Yale law professor Anne Alstott argues, justifying parental support depends on defining the family as a social good that, in some sense, society must pay for.

正如耶鲁大学法律教授Anne Alstott认为的,要证明父母的养育是合理的取决于要把家庭定义为一个好的社会事物,从某些意义上来说,社会必须有所付出。

justified ['dʒʌstɪfɪd] adj. 合理的；理所应当的 15613
搭配:justified concern:合理的担心
be wholly justified:……是完全合理的
be absolutely justified in doing sth:完全有理由做某事

justification [dʒʌstɪfɪ'keɪʃ(ə)n] n. 正当的理由；为……辩护 5898
搭配:contrive various justifications:设计出各种各样理由
no justification for(doing)sth:有/没有做……事情的理由
in justification(of sb/sth):为(某人/某事)辩解

释义:(N\-VAR)正当理由；合理的解释

A justification for something is an acceptable reason or explanation for it.
写作例句:有人认为要求回报是合理的,其依据是助人者会花费时间和精力。
Some justify requiring something in return on the ground that the benefactor will spend time and efforts in it.

Some hold that asking for compensation is justified on the ground the benefactor will spend time and efforts in it.

Some offer justifications for asking something in return on the ground that the benefactor will spend time and efforts in it.

justifiable ['dʒʌstɪ'faɪəb(ə)l] adj. (行为、反应、决定等］有道理的；可证明是正当的；情有可原的 15950
搭配:justifiable anger:情有可原的愤怒
justifiable pride:无可非议的自豪感
economically/commercially justifiable:经济上/商业上合理的

释义:(ADJ-GRADED)有理由的；无可非议的；情有可原的
An action, situation, emotion, or idea that is justifiable is acceptable or correct because there is a good reason for it.

justifiably ['dʒʌstɪfaiəbli] adv. 有理由地；无可非议地 18390

jury ['dʒʊərɪ] n. 陪审团；(竞赛的)评委会 1660

词源:来自拉丁语iurare: 发誓; 誄言。来自ius: 法律。即以誓言保证公正审判的人, 引申词义陪审团。
助记: ju- (= judge: 审判)+ ry → (法律)陪审团
搭配: the jury is out/the jury is still out: 尚无定论

jury trial: 陪审团审案

词源: late 14c., "act of swearing to a statement known to be false," via Anglo-French perjorie (late 13c.)and Old French parjurée "perjury, false witness," both from Latin periurium "a false oath," from periurare "swear falsely". Related: Perjurious.

词源:来自盎格鲁-诺曼语perjurie,来自拉丁语periurare(=swear falsely:发假誓),来自拉丁语per- + jurare。
助记:per-(=away:离开)+ jury(=to swear:发誓)→离开正确的誓言,发错误的假誓→伪证；伪誓；伪证罪
搭配:commit perjury:犯伪证罪；发假誓

guilty of perjury:伪证罪
助记:来自jury(陪审团)+-ist(人)即陪审团成员；有法律知识的人→引申词义法学家；法律专家
搭配:civil jurist:民法学家
助记:来自拉丁语iuris(法律的)+ 拉丁语prudentia(知识；实践智慧)→来自拉丁语iurisprudentia(法律的科学；法律的知识)→引申词义法学
搭配:medical jurisprudence:法医学
criminal Jurisprudence:刑法学
助记:in-(否定)+jure(司法；法律)→不遵守法律→干伤天害理的事情→伤害；损害(v.)
搭配:be badly/seriously/critically injured: 深受重伤
injure sb's pride/feelings etc.: 伤害某人的自尊/情感等
在日常英语中,人们一般说hurt,而不说injure。如hurt the leg: 伤了腿；hurt my feelings: 伤害了我的感情。

injury ['ɪn(d)ʒ(ə)rr] n. (身体上的)损害[+to]；(对某人名誉、事业或情感的)伤害[+to] 1562
搭配:cause serious injury to his reputation:使他的名誉受到了严重损害

injured ['ɪndʒəd] adj. 受伤的；受伤者；(感情)受伤害的 5592
搭配: the injured: 伤者

injured look/expression etc.: 委屈的样子/表情等

a look of injured pride: 自尊心受伤的表情

conjure ['kʌndʒə] vt.&vi. 变魔术 vt. 使(某物)突然出现[发生] 7876

词源:从13世纪开始,这个词逐渐衍生出魔幻含义,意为“通过咒语召唤神鬼、驱使神鬼”。人们认为,巫师或魔法师通过念咒的方式来召集鬼魂,其实就是在与神鬼密谋,以发誓诅咒的方式请求神鬼的协助,所以conjure一词产生了“念咒召唤神鬼”的意思。后来,逐渐演变处“变魔术”,“凭空变出；想象出”的含义。
搭配:conjure a rabbit out of hat:从帽子里变出一只兔子来
conjure victories from bad situations:从糟糕的环境中出人意料地取得胜利
conjure up:使如变魔术般凭空出现；想起,使在脑海中显现

![](images/5464dfe8c8ff5d69a0c36944b30a7f87b981ac18fa8a4d28d945ecc3440bc157.jpg)

adjust [ə'dʒʌst] vt.&vi. 调整以适应 vt. 调整；调节；适应 2320
助记:ad-(=to)+just(刚好；合适)→去适合→使……适合；调整……以适应
搭配:adjust A to B:调整A 以适应B(=adapt A to B)

adjust themselves to civil society:进行自我调整以适应普通社会

adjust its tax and labor laws:调整了其税务及劳动法规

adjust the mirror:调节了后视镜

adjust his vision to the faint starlight: 使眼睛适应昏暗的星光

例句:1)Our kids need to adjust to that, but too much pushiness can be destructive.

我们的孩子必须去调整以适应那个,但是过多的逼迫可能会带来毁灭性的后果。

2)And global warming could wipe out species unable to quickly adapt to changing climate/circumstance/environment.

全球变暖可能会消灭那么不能很快适应变化环境的物种。

![](images/83341d47a8ad2521c1476831cdaf90b87a4c0408c8071cf48ae06c1848fe838c.jpg)

搭配: adjustable shoulder straps: 可调肩带

adjustment [ə'dʒʌs(t)m(ə)nt] n. (对机器、做事方法等的)调整；(对行为、思想等的)调整 3146
搭配:adjustments to taxation:调税
after adjustment for inflation:在通货膨胀调整后
make major adjustments to his thinking:对他的思维方式作大的调整
poor adjustment to seasonal change:很差的调节适应季节变化的能力
写作例句:当不幸的事情发生时,我们应该及时调整心态去适应它。

When something unfortunate happens, we should adjust our mentality to it timely.

When something bad takes place, we should adapt ourselves to it in time. When something miserable occurs, we should make some adjustments to it immediately.

搭配:adapt to the change:适应变化

搭配: the adaptability of wool: 羊毛的适应性

词根“opt- to desire, choose, grab, take”,含义为想要；选择；夺取；获得。同样表达选择的词根还有“op-”等。

词源: From optare "to desire, pray for, choose," which is of uncertain origin.

De Vaan derives it from Proto-Italic *opeje- "to choose, grab," from PIE *hopeie- "to choose, grab," and compares Hittite epp/app- "to take, grab," Sanskrit apa, Avestanapa "has reached."

opt [ɒpt] vt.&vi. 选择 4755
搭配:opt for one method or the other:选择这种或那种方法
opt out:选择不参加

"opt-"的派生词有option, optional, co-opt, adopt, adopted, adoption, adoptive等。

option ['ɒpʃ(ə)n] n. 供选择的东西；选择权；购买权；出售权；期权；选修课 1106

词源: c. 1600, "action of choosing;" 1630s, "power or liberty of choosing," from French option (Old French option), from Latin optionem (nominative optio)"choice, free choice, liberty to choose".

The meaning "thing that may be chosen" is attested from 1885. The commercial transaction sense of "privilege secured by payment of a premium (on a stock or a certain produce at a specified time and at a specified price)is recorded from 1755 (the verb in this sense is from 1934). As a North American football play in which the back may either pass the ball or run with it, it is recorded from 1954.
搭配: have the option of: 有……的选择

keep your options open/leave your options open: 暂不做决定

optional ['ɒpʃ(ə)n(ə)l] adj. 可选择的 5770
搭配:take optional courses:上选修课

co-opt [kəʊ'ɔpt] vt. 团结；指派；借鉴 14445
搭配:try to co-opt rather than defeat his critics:试着团结而非打击批评他的人

be co-opted into the Labor Government: 被指派加入了工党政府
co-opt many nationalist slogans: 借鉴了很多民族主义的口号

adopt [ə'dɒpt] vt. 采纳；采用(态度/方式等)vt.&vi. 收养 1641
助记:ad-(=to:去)+opt(=choose, wish, desire:选择；希望)→选择然后采用→采纳；采取(即:“选择”什么)

ad-(=to:去)+opt(=choose, wish, desire:选择；希望)→选择然后领走→收养(即:“选择”一个孩子养)
搭配:adopt a new technique/policy:采取一种新的技术/政策

adopt black children:收养黑人小孩

adopt an approach/policy/attitude etc.:采用某种方法/政策/态度等

adopted [ə'dɒptɪd] adj. 领养的；〔国家〕选择移居的 10808
搭配:adopted country:移居的国家

adoption [ə'dɒpʃ(ə)n] n. 领养；采纳；〔候选人的〕提名,推选 3711 搭配: his adoption as the Labour candidate: 他被选定为工党候选人

adoptive [ə'dɒptɪv] adj. 收养的(家庭)11032
搭配:adoptive parents:养父母

"opine" 表示 "认为","opinion" 表示 "看法；意见"。

opine [ə(u)'pain] vt.&vi. 认为；发表意见 17585

词源:mid-15c., opinen, "express an opinion or opinions; to think, suppose," also transitive, "be of the opinion that," from Old French oppiner, opiner (15c.)and directly from Latin opinari "have an opinion, be of opinion, suppose, conjecture, think, judge". 来自拉丁语opinari, 发表观点, 表达意见。
搭配: opine that...: 认为……

opinion [ə'pɪnjən] n. 看法；评价；舆论；(专家的)意见 1127
助记:它来自拉丁语opinionem(意见；主张),最终来自印欧词根op-“选择”。你所坚执的主张、评价、看法,民众形成的舆论,是你或民众自己选择的结果。
搭配:in sb's opinion:据……的意见

someone is of the opinion that:某人持……的观点

public opinion:民意；公众舆论

词根 “guar-, gard=guard=watch=ward”,含义为护卫；保护；留意。

词源: Because g- followed by some vowels in English usually has a "soft" pronunciation, a silent -u- sometimes was inserted between the g- and the vowel in Middle English to signal hardness, especially in words from French; but this was not done with many Scandinavian words where hard "g" precedes a vowel (gear, get, give, etc.). Germanic -w- generally became -gu- in words borrowed into Romance languages, but Old North French preserved the Frankish -w-, and English sometimes borrowed both forms, hence guarantee/warranty, guard/ward, etc.

guard [gɑːd] n. 守卫；保护；看守 n. 卫兵；防护装置；列车员 1291
助记:guard(=watch:守护；留意)→保卫；留意；警惕
搭配:guard against:防止:提防

guard their territory:保卫他们的领土

catch sb off guard: 乘某人不备使其大吃一惊

lower your guard/let your guard down/drop your guard: 放松警惕

on one's guard or on guard: 警惕；值守

stand guard: 站岗

例句:Data is becoming an asset which needs to be guarded as much as any other asset.

数据正在变成一种资产．和其他资产一样需要被保护。

仿写例句:知识产权也是一种资产,和其他有形资产一样需要被保护。

Intellectual property is an asset which needs to be guarded/protected as much as other tangible asset.

![](images/8a1f8a6b736c68621152d75bea9c9e0e42cacf5a2e1af50cec949caa720edfd9.jpg)

guard 的同义词是 ward:

ward [wɔ:d] n. 病房；选区；被监护人〔尤指儿童〕 vi. 5防止；抵挡〔疾病、危险或攻击等〕127
搭配:ward sth. off: 防止；抵挡某物

![](images/ec37af4de3d9e3b38a5f9e07129122fee9622055ce9d5e549d1f6c57c766e264.jpg)

guard的派生词有guarded,safeguard,regard,disregard,regardless,regarding 等。

guarded ['gɑːdɪd] adj. 谨慎的；有保留的；提防的 13827

safeguard ['seɪfgɑːd] n. 保护；保卫；保护措施 9317
助记:safe(安全)+guard(保卫；保护)→保护...的安全；保护
搭配:safeguard the interests of animals:保护动物利益

regard [ri'ga:d] n. 注意；关心[+for]；尊敬[+for]；表良好祝愿(复数)vt. 认为,看作；(以某种方式)注视 2101
助记:re-(表加强语气)+gard(=look, watch=heed: 注意；留心)→注意；关心；看作；注视
搭配: regard A as B: 把A认作B

lightly regarded: 不被重视; 不被留意

Jan's regard for his great talent: 简对他卓越才能的敬佩

little/no/scant regard (for sb/sth): 对……关注很少

as regards to: 至于

with regard to/in regard to: 有关

例句:One feature of a good grading system is that those measured by it generally regard it as fair and reasonable—not the case here.

一个良好的评分系统的特征之一是被评价的人普遍都将它看作是公平的和合理的,而不是现在这个情况。
助记:dis-(=not, opposite of: 不；相反)+regard(关心；留意)→不留意:不关心→对……置之不理；忽视
搭配:disregard of water safety rules:不管水质安全规定

regardless [rɪ'gɑːdlɪs] adv. 不顾一切地 2922
助记:regard(关心；留意)+less(表否定)→不留意→不顾一切地
搭配: regardless of: 不管; 无论

例句:At any rate this change will ultimately be acclaimed by an ever-growing number of both domestic and international consumers regardless of how long the current consumer pattern will take hold.

阅读难点:at any rate:无论如何(=anyhow= in any case = on all accounts)

acclaim [ə'kleim] v. 称颂；称赞；喝彩

take hold:扛着:持续

仿写例句:无论如何,不管互联网对交际的影响会持续多久,这个变革都值得人们永远记住。

At any rate/Anyhow/In any case/On all accounts this revolutionary change deserves remembering forever regardless of how long its effect will take hold.

regarding [rɪ'gɑːdɪŋ] prep. 关于〔尤用于信函或演说中〕2172
助记:regard(与……有关)+ing→关于；就……而言
搭配:questions regarding job-hunting:关于找工作的问题

guarantee [ˈgærənˈtiː] vt. 确保；保证……必定发生；担保 n. 保证；保修单；担保物 2798
助记:guar- (=guard: 保卫; 守卫)+-ant(名词后缀)+ee→保证；担保
搭配:be far from guaranteed: 难以保障
guaranteed payment: 有保障的回报
a guarantee of quality: 保证质量

a guarantee of returning to do their military service: 作为回来服兵役的担保

例句:Degrees of prestigious universities do not guarantee entry to graduate programs.

名校(本科)学历并不能确保进入到研究生计划。

仿写例句:大量的证书并不能确保进入到一个名企。

A mass of/A great many/A large number of/Multitudes of/A large quantity of certificates do not guarantee entry to famous/prestigious companies/corporations.

guaranteed ['gærən'tɪd] adj. 肯定的；保证的 9264
搭配:be guaranteed to cause anxiety:肯定会引起焦虑

guarantee 的同义词为 warrant 和 pledge,都有担保；保证的含义。

warrant ['wɔːrəntɪ] vt. 保证；保护；使……显得必要/适当 n. 搜查令；拘捕令 6154
助记:warrant (=guarant:保护；保证)→safeguard, protect; guarantee, pledge: 保证；保护→引申义为使……显得必要/适当；搜查令；拘捕令(搜查、逮捕有法律保护)
搭配: to warrant an investigation: 有必要进行一番调查
 arrest warrant: 逮捕证

warranty ['wɒr(ə)ntri] n. (产品的)保用证；保修单 9807
搭配:still under warranty:还在保修期内

unwarranted [ʌn'wɒr(ə)ntrɪd] adj. 不必要的；无端的 15815
搭配:an unwarranted interference in the country's internal affairs:对该国内政的无端干涉

pledge [pledʒ] vt. 保证(做某事)；保证给予(某物)；承诺支付(一笔款)；抵押 n. 誳言；承诺拨款 5262
助记:pledg (=guard: 保证；保卫)+e→保证；许诺；誓言
搭配:pledge of the Declaration of Independence: 独立宣言的承诺

pledge $150 million in French aid: 承诺拨款1.5亿美元用于法国援助

pledge to support: 保证支持……

pledge himself to increase taxes for the rich: 保证增加富人税收

garage ['gɑːrdʒɪ'gɑːrɪdʒ] n. 车库；汽车修理厂 vt. 将(汽车)开进[停放在]车库 3237

词源:日耳曼语族中的w在罗曼语系中会变为g(u)-。史前日耳曼语war-(看管,看护,与英语ward, warn, beware同源)被古法语(属于罗曼语系)借用为动词garer(停船于船坞,防护,保护),在法语中派生了名词garage,被英语和德语等借用为现代的意义。
搭配:underground garage:地下车库

garment ['gɑːm(ə)nt] n. 衣服(尤用于衣服生产和销售的领域)6195

词源:来自词根wer-,保护,隐藏。词源同warrant,后指衣服。
助记:gar-(=wer-:保护；遮蔽)+-ment(名词后缀)→其保护遮蔽作用的衣服
搭配:garment industry:制农业

garnish [ˈgɑːnɪʃ] n. 装饰菜 vt. 加饰菜于 9691

词源:来自法语。来自词根wer-,保护,隐藏。词源同warrant。后指装饰。
搭配:a garnish of chopped raw onion, tomato, and fresh coriander:剁碎的生洋葱、西红柿和新鲜香菜做成的装饰菜

garnish the roast:给烤肉配饰菜

garrison ['gærɪs(ə)n] n. 卫戍部队；卫戍区 vt. 派兵驻守 14498

词源:耳曼语族中的w在罗曼语系中会变为g(u)。来自wer-,保护,防御,词源同warrant。原指城堡守卫,后指卫戍部队。史前日耳曼语

war-(看管；看护)产生了warjan(保护；防护),被古法语(属于罗曼语系)借用为garir,派生了garison(保护；防护),被英语借用为garrison。
搭配:garrison the country:驻守这个国家

词根“wer- to cover”,表示“保护；覆盖”。“wer-”词根的变体有“ward- guar-:保护”。

词源: It is the hypothetical source of/evidence for its existence is provided by: Sanskrit vatah "enclosure," vrnoti "covers, wraps, shuts;" Lithuanian užveriu, užverti "to shut, to close;" Old Persian *pari-varaka "protective;" Latin (op)erire "to cover," (ap)erire "open, uncover" (with ap- "off, away"); Old Church Slavonic vora "sealed, closed," vreti "shut;" Old Irish feronn "field," properly "enclosed land;" Old English wer "dam, fence, enclosure," German Wehr "defense, protection," Gothic warjan "to defend, protect."

词根 “ward- to guard” 一般表示 “保护；保护”

ward [wɔ:d] n. 病房；选区；被监护人〔尤指儿童〕 vi. 5防止；抵挡〔疾病、危险或攻击等〕127
助记:ward(=guard:保卫；防止)→避免；防止；抵挡
搭配:ward off terrorist suspects at the border:把恐怖分子嫌疑犯挡在边境外
ward off the mosquitoes:防蚊

例句:Religious associations began, for example, in the desire to secure the favor of overruling powers and to ward off evil influences.

比如,宗教社团的开始产生是为了获得神灵恩赐,阻挡邪恶势力。

写作例句:互联网的产生是为了确保信息能够得到最大化的分享,防止造成数字分化。

The Internet began in the desire to secure the information can be shared fully/maximumly and to ward off/prevent digital divide.

(数字分化指的是世界被分成了信息富裕区域和信息贫穷区域)

warden ['wɔ:d(ə)n] n. 管理人[+of]；典狱官；(法律、法规)督察员 9548
搭配:forest/park etc. warden:护林员/公园管理员等

the warden of the college:学院的院长

warn [wɔːn] vt.&vi. 警告；提醒；告诫 1786

词源:来此词根wer-:覆盖；保护；看管；看护→引申词义提醒；警告；告诫。
搭配:warn sb not to do sth:警告不要做某事
warn against:警告……不要

warning [ˈwɔːnɪŋ] n. 警告；预告 adj. 警告性的 2120

cover ['kʌvə] vt. 盖住；覆盖；铺盖；走过(一段距离)；保险；适用于；论及；足够支付 vi. 包庇；代替 n. 套子；封面；掩护；掩蔽处 n. (保险)保障；掩护；床上盖具 561

助记:un-(reverse of: 相反；逆向)+cover(盖子)→拿去盖子→揭露；发现

coverage ['kʌv(ə)rɪdʒ] n. 新闻报道；保险范围；(书、节目、课程等的)内容范围[+ of] 1890

covertly ['kʌvətli] adv. 偷偷摸摸地；秘密地 20073

curfew ['kɜːfjuː] n. 宵禁；熄灯令；〔父母规定的〕儿童晚上必须回家[睡觉]的时间 10715

词源: 来自古法语cuevrefeu, 来自cuevr, 同cover, 遮盖, feu, 同focus, 火, 火炉, 焦点。

中世纪在欧洲某些地区法令规定一到夜间某个时刻晚钟敲响之后就得灭火熄灯就寝。公元1066年操法语的诺曼人征服了英国, 1068年威廉一世下令将打晚钟的时刻定为8时。晚间定时灭火熄灯就寝的这

一规定,“灭火熄灯”就寝的这种晚钟就是curfew一词的原始意义。究其根源curfew并非固有的英语词,它源自古法语couvrefew ‘coverfire’。我们如今使用的curfew已不再作此义解,其词义已引申为“戒严”,“宵禁”。
搭配:be placed under curfew:处于宵禁之中
before the nine o'clock curfew:在9点熄灯之前

discover [dr'skʌvə] vt. (首次)发现；发觉 959
助记:dis-(=opposite of: 表相反)+cover(盖)→揭去盖子→发现；发觉

discover 的派生词有 discovery, rediscover, undiscovered 等。

discovery [dr'skʌv(ə)rɪ] n. 被发现的事实[事物][+about]；发现[+of] 2247

the discovery of oil in Alaska:在阿拉斯加发现石油

undiscovered [ʌndɪ'skʌvəd] adj. 未找到(或注意到)的；未被发现的 17888
搭配:a previously undiscovered talent:以前没被发掘的天才

mask [mɑːsk] n. 面具；伪装；面膜 vt. 掩饰；遮盖；盖住(气味、味道、声音等)2917
搭配:mask of detachment:超然的伪装

mask the enemy: 遮住敌人

但是,全国数据掩盖了各大学表现之间的巨大差异。

protect [prə'tekt] vt.&vi. 保护；防护 vt. 为……提供保险(一般用作被动语态)；(通过征收关税或限制进口商品)保护(国内工商业)750
助记:来自pro-(=in front of: 在前面)+ -tect(=-teg=to cover: 遮盖；覆盖)→to protect, cover in front: 保护；在前面盖住→保护；防护→扩展含义为……提供保险；(通过征收关税或限制进口商品)保护(国内工商业)
搭配: be partially protected: 得到部分保险保障

protect the machine from dust: 防止灰尘落进机器

protect的派生词有protector, protected, protective, unprotected, protection, protectionist, protectionism 等。

unprotected [ʌnprə'tektɪd] adj. (人或地方)未受保护的, 未设防的; 暴露在外的; 易受损的; 未用避孕套的 12161
助记: un- (=not: 不)+protected (受保护的)→不受保护的→(人或地方)未受保护的; 暴露在外的; 未用避孕套的
搭配: unprotected landing beaches: 无设防的登陆海滩

助记:protect(保护)+-ion(名词后缀)→保护；保险；保护法；贸易保护；保护费
搭配:provide protection for our children:为孩子们提供保护

protectionist [prəʊ'tekʃnɪst] n. 贸易保护主义者 adj. (政策、措施、法律)

贸易保护主义的 18208
助记:protection(贸易保护)+-ist(名词后缀,表示人；形容词后缀,表示……主义的)→贸易保护主义者；(政策、措施、法律)贸易保护

笔记区

主义的
搭配:protectionist policies:保护主义政策

释义:(N-COUNT)贸易保护主义者

A protectionist is someone who agrees with and supports protectionism.

Protectionist policies, measures, and laws are meant to stop or reduce imports.

protectionism [prə'tek'ənɪzəm] n. 贸易保护主义 16702
助记:protection(贸易保护)+-ism(名词后缀,表主义)→贸易保护主义
搭配:avert increasing protectionism:遏制贸易保护主义抬头

释义:(N-UNCOUNT)贸易保护主义

Protectionism is the policy some countries have of helping their own industries by putting a large tax on imported goods or by restricting imports in some other way.

protégé [ˈprɒtəʒər] n. 门徒；受提携的后进者 14624

词源: 1778, from French protégé (fem. protégée)“one who is protected,” noun use of past participle of Middle French protéger “protect,” from Latin protegere (see protect; also see protection).
助记:protégé=one who is protected:被保护的人→门徒；受提携的后进者
搭配:a protégé of the great violinist Yehudi Menuhin:伟大的小提琴家耶胡迪·梅纽因的门生

释义:(NOUN)(来自法语,受提携的后进者)

Protégé is a young person who is helped in their career and personal development by a more experienced person

![](images/44ba732583a4d4e2c1c7236a789e747b873a907d424cacfadb9eccbd57d0fbb0.jpg)

同样表达遮掩含义的单词还有 obscure。

obscure [əb'skjuə] adj. 鲜为人知的；复杂难懂的；不清楚的 vt. 遮掩；使……难懂 5938
助记:ob- (=over: 上面)+scure (=to cover, conceal: 遮盖；隐藏)→遮盖在头顶,隐藏→模糊不清的→引申义为遮掩；使……难懂；鲜为人知的；复杂难懂的
搭配:obscure his vision:遮住了他的视线

obscure glass: 毛玻璃

obscure language: 复杂难懂的语言

obscure origin: 鲜为人知的起源

例句:But these successes paradoxically obscure the tremendous human costs of historically accumulated disadvantage that remain central to black Americans' lives.

矛盾的是,这些成功掩盖了历史上不断累积的不利的巨大人力成本,这依然是美国黑人生活的重心。

![](images/36c940119697a2e16ba135b177a7ed94b78ab5685b81587a71fcf0b6d1d89c60.jpg)

obscure 的派生词是 obscurity 等。

obscurity [əb'skiuərɪtɪ] n. 默默无闻；难懂之物 12804
搭配:pluck from obscurity:从默默无闻中脱颖而出
the obscurity of reply:费解的回答

shell [ʃel] n. (坚果或蛋的)壳；壳料；(动物的)甲壳；贝壳；矜持；框架；炮弹；炮击 vt. 剥……的壳；炮击 2582
助记:shell(=cover:盖,掩盖物；词根部分)→壳；贝壳(即:“掩盖”住动物身体的东西)
搭配:shell out:付款:花钱

shell and ate a few nuts:剥了一些坚果吃

shell the densely-populated suburbs near the port: 炸弹击了港口附近人口稠密的郊区

come out of one's shell:开始活跃起来

in the shell:尚未成熟,在酝酿之中

例句:Facing their children's complaints of "nothing to do", parents were shelling out large numbers of dollars for various forms of entertainment.

面对他们孩子觉得无事可做的抱怨,父母们花了大量的钱去各种娱乐。

仿写例句:面对孩子觉得负担过重的抱怨,父母并没有同情,相反,他们还花大量的钱把孩子送去上各种艺术班。

Facing/Confronting their children's complaints of excessive burden, parents did not show any sign of sympathy. On the contrary, they shelled out a large amount of money for various art classes.

![](images/4c8c58588c70f7937dd602dd949ea9dbb4378387073ef89a11dbaec6eac2b295.jpg)

shell 的派生词是 shellfish, shelling, bombshell, nutshell 等

shellfish ['ʃelfɪʃ] n. 有壳的水生动物；甲壳类动物 13497

shield [ʃɪːld] n. 防护物；保护人；盾；盾形奖章 vt. 保护；遮挡 5678
助记:shiel(=shell:壳,贝壳)+d(无意义)→防护物；保护,防护(因为“壳“就是动物的“防护物”,起到“保护”的作用)
搭配:the wind-shields:挡风玻璃

![](images/7669031c67b047e2952fd0108aed4324808c54462bbe7e5f6a343aeca2443b59.jpg)

shelter ['ʃeltə] n. 躲避处；遮蔽；庇护；收容所 vi. 躲避 vt. 遮蔽；庇护 2896

sheltered ['ʃeltəd] adj. (地方)受掩护的,免遭恶劣天气影响的；收呵护的；福利性的(住所或工作)13665

![](images/e7657349ff594383714786409a59e258f69d452fc1162d400694315607d4e4a4.jpg)

有时词根“ward”也表示“方向；朝向”

词源: adverbial suffix expressing direction, Old English -weard "toward," literally "turned toward," sometimes -weardes, with genitive singular ending of neuter adjectives, from Proto-Germanic *werda- (cognates: Old Saxon, Old Frisian -ward, Old Norse -verðr), variant of PIE *werto- "to turn, wind," from root *wer- (2)"to turn, bend." The original notion is of "turned toward."

inward ['ɪnwəd] adj. 内心的；向内的 adv. 向内地 11469
助记:in-(向里；在内)+ -ward(朝向；方向)→朝向向内→内心的；向内的
搭配:a sharp, inward breath like a gasp:像倒抽气一样急速吸入的一口气
sigh with inward relief:内心释然地长出了一口气
inward investment:对内投资

inwardly ['mwa:dlɪ] adv.(思想、情感或行为)在内心；在心灵深处 17959
搭配:inwardly furious:内心异常愤怒

onward ['ɒnwəd] adj. 向前的；(旅程)继续进行的；发展的 adv. 向前地；(旅程)继续进行地；发展地；从……以后(outwards)12466

outward ['aʊtwəd] adj. 表面看来的；外在的；外出的 adv. 向外(移动)地；(面)向外地；向外(看)地 8761
搭配:outwardly calm:表面上平静

toward [tə'wɔ:d] prep. 向；趋向；对于…；接近(时间)；靠近；(钱)用于 385
助记:to(朝向)+-ward(表方向)→趋向；接近；靠近
搭配:a major step toward peace:走向和平的一大步

go toward the eastern shore:靠近东海岸

attitude toward religion:对宗教的态度

towards [tə'wɔ:dz; twɔ:dz; 'tɔ:dz] prep. 朝, 向; 接近; 关于; 以……为目标 (或目的); 用于 2018
搭配:towards the end of April:将近四月底

go towards a new school building: (资金)用于修建新校舍

upward ['ʌpwəd] adj. 向上的；朝上的；(数量、价格)上升的；上涨的；增长的 6240
助记:up(向上)+ward(朝向)→向上的；朝上的；上升的
搭配:an upward gaze:举目凝望

an upward movement in property prices:房地产价格的上升

upwards ['ʌpwədz] adv. 向上；向高处；(数量、价格)上涨；超过(\~of sth )11275
搭配:pay upwards of £50:预计至少支付50英镑

downward ['daunwəd] adj. 下降的；向下的；逐渐下降的；日趋恶化的 adv. 朝下地；下降地；往下地 8419

eastward ['i:stwəd] adj. 向东的 adv. 向东地 14709
助记:east(东)+ -ward(朝向)→向东朝向→向东的；向东地
搭配:move eastward:向东移动

the eastward expansion of the city:该市的东扩

westward ['westwəd] adj. 向西的 adv. 向西 12923

搭配: sail westward: 向西航行

the one-hour westward flight: 一个小时的向西飞行

southward ['sauθwəd] adj. 向南的 adv. 向南 17377
助记: south(南)+ -ward(朝向)→向南朝向→向南的；向南地
搭配: drive southward: 向南驶去

southward course: 向南去的路

northward ['nɔːθwəd] adj. 向北的 adv. 向北 14631
助记: north(北)+ -ward(朝向)→向北朝向→向北的；向北地
搭配: push northward up Florida's coast: 沿着佛罗里达海岸向北推进

the northward journey: 向北的行程

afterwards [ˈa:fəwədz] adv. 随后；后来 5728
搭配: shortly afterwards: 不久之后

years afterwards: 此后多年

forward ['fɔːwəd] adv. 向前；进展；向将来 adj. 向前的 vt. 转寄；发送；促进 n. (足球、篮球等运动的)前锋 818
搭配:look forward:期待
forward planning/thinking:预先计划/提前考虑
a good chance to forward my career:促进我事业发展的一个好机会

forwards ['fɔːwədz] adv 向前；进展；向将来 15886

skyward ['skaiwəd] adv. 朝向天空 15939
助记: sky(天空)+ -ward(朝向)→朝向天空
搭配: point skywards: 指向天空

wayward ['weɪwəd] adj. 任性的；倔强的 14754
助记: way- (=away: 离开)+ -ward (=to turn: 转身)→ turn away: 转身离开 (按照自己的意思走)→引申词义人性的；倔强的
搭配: a wayward teenager: 任性的少年

coward ['kauəd] n. 胆小鬼, 懦夫; 胆小的
助记:co(=tail:尾巴)+ward(向)→(遇到事情)就走向(某人)尾巴后面→胆小的；胆小鬼

awkward ['ɔːkwəd] adj. 令人尴尬的；(使用)不便的；棘手的(工作)；笨拙的；难为情的 5053

词源: Mid-14c. (adv.), "in the wrong direction". As an adjective, "turned the wrong way," 1510s. Meaning "clumsy, wanting ease and grace in movement" recorded by 1520s. Of persons, the meaning "embarrassed, ill-at-ease" is from 1713s. Related: Awkwardly.
助记:awk(=back:背的,背后的)+ward(表方向性:向)→向后面的,向背后的→不顺手的(即:用手不好处理的),难操纵的；笨拙的,不灵活的→引申义为令人尴尬的；棘手的；难为情的
搭配:an awkward gesture:一个笨拙的手势
feel awkward:感觉到别扭,尴尬

例句:If you feel awkward being humorous, you must practice so that it becomes more natural.

如果你在幽默的时候感到尴尬,你必须练习一下以至于能够更自然一些。

awkwardly ['ɔːkwɔːdli] adv. 笨拙地；无技巧地 10886
搭配: awkward questions:尴尬的问题
make it awkward to carry:不便携带
an awkwardly long silence:一段令人尴尬的长时间的沉默
feel awkward doing sth:做某事让人感到难为情

awkwardness ['ɔkwədnɪs] n. 尴尬；笨拙 17966
搭配:cover up her awkwardness:掩饰她的尴尬

但有时词根 “ward” 也表示 to grant, bestow, 表示 “奖励, 回报”

reward [ri'wɔ:d] n. 回报；报酬；奖赏；悬赏金[+of] vt. 酬谢；奖赏；获得奖励 3420
助记:reward(=repay:回报；报答)→回报；奖赏；获得奖励
搭配:rewards and punishments:奖惩

reward them for behaving well:奖励他们表现好

a reward of $20,000:2万美元悬赏金

substantial rewards:巨额回报

rewarding [rɪ'wɔ:dɪŋ] adj. 令人满意的；令人有所收获的 9525
搭配:a rewarding career:令人有所收获的工作

例句:There aren't many jobs in science for them, so they go to Wall Street and Silicon Valley to apply their analytical skills to more practical—and rewarding—efforts.

因为在科学领域没有足够的工作给他们,所以他们走向华尔街和硅谷去做更加实用——以及报酬更加丰厚——的工作。

award [ə'wɔ:d] vt. 被授予；给予 n. 奖；(赔偿金等的)裁定额 2596
助记:a-(加强语气)+-ward (=reward: 奖励)→奖品, 奖励; 授予搭配: be awarded doctoral degrees: 被授予博士学位
award the contract to a company: 将合同给予一家公司
worker's compensation awards: 工人的赔偿金裁定额
annual award: 年度奖

award-winning [ə'wɔ:d'wɪnɪŋ] adj. 获奖的 9401
搭配:an award-winning photo journalist:一位获奖的摄影记者
his award-winning film:他的获奖电影

![](images/20c6997f93d3e328f585c862ae90b869ef6c4235248fe70ffad8dd0cff486c2f.jpg)

类比,同样表达奖金；奖品的单词还有 premium。

premium ['prɪmɪəm] n. 保险费；额外费用 adj. 优质的；高端的；以高价(买、卖)
搭配: place a premium on: 看重; 重视
at a premium: 求之难得/
premium price/rate: 高价/高利率
premium quality British potatoes: 优质英国马铃薯

: As a consequence, we have truly entered the Post-Industrial economy. We are rapidly shifting from an economy based on manufacturing and commodities to one that places the greatest value on information, services, support, and distribution. That shift, in turn, place an unprecedented premium on "knowledge workers," a new class of wealthy, educated, and mobile people who view themselves as free agents in a seller's market.

其结果是, 我们正正进入到一个后工业经济中。我们正快速从基于制造业和商品的经济转变成最重视信息, 服务, 支持和分销的经济。这种转变反过来又史无前例地重视知识型工人, 这个新的富有的, 受过良好教育的和流动性阶级将他们自己视为在一个卖方市场中自由从业者。

阅读难点:shift from A to B:从A转变成B
place value on:重视 in turn:反过来

place an unprecedented premium on:史无前例的重视

仿写例句:结果是,我们进入到一个数字化产品时代。我们正快速从基于生产和商品的经济转变成重视科技,信息和服务的经济。这个转变反过来又前所未有地重视知识型工人,这个阶级的人受过良好教育,他们不看重证书,只重视能力。

As a consequence, we have truly entered the digital-product era/age. We are rapidly shifting from an economy based on manufacturing and commodities to one that place great value on technology, information and service. This shift, in turn, place an unprecedented premium on "knowledge workers", a class of well-educated people who attach great importance to abilities/capacities/capabilities and think little of certificates.

复习:“重视”表达方式:

pay attention to; lay emphasis on/upon=emphasize; attach importance to
place value(价值n.)on/upon=value(重视v.); think highly of: 高度
重视、认同

place a premium on: 重视；押宝

![](images/9c966ec1188ffd74cfc903ff48dd8b85319c9dfd2d5e7a38023c494c676674e7.jpg)

cure 的含义为治愈,解决；解决方法。

cure [kjuə; kjɔː] vt. 治愈(疾病、病人)；解决；加工处理 n. (有治愈效果的)药物、疗法；解决方法[+for] 4633

词源: vt. late 14c., "to restore to health or a sound state," from Old French curer and directly from Latin curare "take care of," hence, in medical language, "treat medically, cure" (see cure (n.1)). In reference to fish, pork, etc., "prepare for preservation by drying, salting, etc.," attested by 1743. Related: Cured; curing.

n. c. 1300, "care, heed," from Latin cura "care, concern, trouble," with many figurative extensions over time such as "study; administration; office of a parish priest; a mistress," and also "means of healing, successful remedial treatment of a disease, medical care" (late 14c.).
助记:来自拉丁语cura,含义为“医疗,照顾”,名词有“治疗方法,成功的治疗方法,医疗护理”等。
搭配:cure the sufferers:治愈患者

a cure for cancer: 一个对癌症治愈方法

incurable [ɪn'kjuərəb(ə)l] adj. 无法治愈的；无可救药的 17938
助记:in-(不；非)+ -cur-(treat medically:医疗)+ -able(形容词后缀,能……的)→无法进行医疗的→无法治愈的；无可救药的
搭配:an incurable romantic:一个无可救药的浪漫主义者
incurable disease:绝症

![](images/c158e6d78bc708f27386a1b31b7f9bf336298a6e7320529782237b0be8dfaef8.jpg)

包含 cure 的单词有 secure, accurate, curious, caution, curator, scour 及其变体。

secure [sɪ'kjuə; sɪ'kjɔː] vt. (尤指经过努力)获得；保护；牢靠地固定 adj. 严密保护的；牢固的；(工作等)稳定的；(感觉)安全的 2511
助记:se- (=free from: 使摆脱；免于)+cure (care: 关心；忧虑)→免于忧虑烦恼的→严密保护的,稳定的,安全的→获得；保护；牢固地固定
搭配:secure happiness:获得幸福
secure the border:确保边境安全
a secure financial situation:一个安全的财务状况

例句:Writer-director Paul Greengrass has gone to great lengths to be respectful in his depiction of what occurred, proceeding with the film only after securing the approval of every victim's family.

编剧兼导演Paul Greengrass已经竭尽全力去使自己的描述忠实于事实,在获得每一位受害者的家属同意之后,他才开始进行电影拍摄。)

securely [sɪ'kɪvəli] adv. 严密保护地；牢固地 12817
搭配:locked the door securely:把门锁好
be securely fixed to:牢牢地固定在……

security [sɪ'kjuərəti] n. 安全措施；安全感；抵押品；有价证券 661
助记:se(=de:表相反)+cur(=care:关心,忧虑)+ity(名词后缀)→不需要关心,忧虑→安全感
搭配:border security:边境安全
a security guard:保安

insecure [ɪnɪsɪ'kjuə(r)] adj. 不自信的；缺乏安全感的；无保障的 10795
搭配:low-paid, insecure jobs: 工资低、无保障的工作

insecurity [ɪnseɪ'kjuərəti] n. 不自信；缺乏安全感 8425
搭配: emotional insecurity: 情感上的不安全感
助记:ac-(=to)+cur-(=care:注意；关注)+ate(形容词后缀)→集中注意力,结果就会更“准确,精准(exact)”(比如考试做题)→精确的；准确的

accurately ['ækjərətli] adv. 精确地；准确地 4950

inaccurate [ɪn'ækjʊrət] adj. 错误的 8868
助记:accura(=accurate:精确的)+cy(名词后缀)→精确；准确
搭配:fire with accuracy at targets:准确无误地射中目标

inaccuracy [ɪn'ækjuːrəsi] n. 不准确 17853

curious ['kjuərɪs] adj. 好奇的；求知欲强的；不寻常的 3139
助记:curi (=care: 关心；好奇)+-ous(形容词后缀)→关心的；好奇的

curiosity [kjuərɪ'ɒsɪtɪ] n. 好奇心；求知欲；奇物；珍品 4570
助记:curi(=curious:好奇的)+-osity(复合名词后缀-ose+-ity,表多的状态)→好奇心；奇物；珍品
搭配:out of curiosity:出于好奇

curiously ['kjuərɪsli] adv. 好奇地 8670

curator [kju(ə)'reitə] n. (博物馆、美术馆的)馆长 6052
助记: cure(看管；经理)+-ator(名词后缀,做……的人)→负责看管、经理的人→引申词义(博物馆、美术馆的)馆长
搭配: curator of fossil fishes:鱼化石的负责人

scour ['skauə] vt. 四处搜索；(费力地)擦洗 n. 擦洗 9727
助记:s+cour (=clean: 干净)→ clean off: 擦去→费力擦洗

搭配: scour the sink: 把水池擦洗干净

caution ['kɔːʃ(ə)n] n. 小心, 谨慎; 警告 vt.&vi. 警告; 告诫 5354
助记: cau (=care, to observe: 小心; 注意)+t(无意义)+-ion(名词后缀)→小心, 谨慎; 警告
搭配: take cautions: 注意, 小心

例句: There is reason for caution but no cause for alarm with regard to food consumption.

考虑到食物消耗, 我们有理由谨慎, 但是没有理由感到恐慌。

阅读难点: with regard to (=with respect to): 关于, 考虑到, 就...而言

仿写例句: 关于食品安全, 我们有理由谨慎, 但是没有理由感到恐慌。

There is reason for caution but no cause for alarm with respect to food safety.

搭配:cautious analysis:谨慎的分析

词源: Also show-down, 1873 in card-playing (especially poker)a slang term for the act of laying down the hands face-up. Figurative sense of "final confrontation" is from 1904.

词源:“warning, hint of caution,” 1550s, Latin, literally “let him beware,” 3rd person singular present subjunctive of cedere “to beware, take heed, watch, guard against,” from PIE root *keu- “to see, observe, perceive.” Legal sense “public warning preventing some action” is from 1650s.
助记: caveat=warning, hint of caution, to beware, guard against: 警告；谨慎；当心；提防

词源:英语单词scavenger来自诺曼时代的英国,特指对外来商品征收税费(scawage)的官员scawager。因这些税务官员同时负责街道清洁的职责,因此,该词又有了拾荒者、食腐动物的含义。
助记:scaveng(=scavenge:拣拾垃圾)+ -er(名词后缀)→捡破烂的人；食腐动物

Sure 含义为 “secure, firm, reliable, safe”,表示 “确定的; 肯定的; 可靠的; 安全的”。

词源: Early 13c., "safe against attack, secure," later "firm, reliable" (c. 1300); "mentally certain, confident" (mid-14c.); "firm, strong, resolute" (c. 1400), from Old French seur, sur "safe, secure; undoubtedly, dependable, trustworthy" (12c.), from Latin securus "free from care, untroubled, heedless, safe".

词根“bi-”“be-”表示“两个；两”,是来自单词“two:两个”。

词源: word-forming element meaning "two, having two, twice, double, doubly, twofold, once every two," etc., from Latin bi- "twice, double," from Old Latin dvi- (cognate with Sanskrit dvi-, Greek di-, dis-, Old English twi-, German zwei- "twice, double"), from PIE root *dwo- "two."

Nativized from 16c. Occasionally bin- before vowels; this form originated in French, not Latin, and might be partly based on or influenced

by Latin bini "twofold" (see binary). In chemical terms, it denotes two parts or equivalents of the substance referred to. Cognate with twi- and di- (1).

bipolar [baɪ'pəʊlə] adj. 完全对立的 10872
助记: bi-(两个)+pole(两级)+ar(形容词后缀)→两极的→完全对立的
搭配: the bipolar world of the Cold War years: 冷战年代的两极世界

binocular [br'nbkju:lə] adj. 双目并用的；双眼的 7757

词源: From French binoculaire, from Latin biniocularis. From biniocus bini "two by two, twofold, two apiece" + ocularis "of the eye".
助记: bin-(bini= two:两个)+ ocular(=of the eye:与眼睛有关的)→双眼的；双目并用的
搭配: binocular vision 双眼视觉

bipartisan [ˈbaɪpɑːtrɪˈzæn] 两党的；两派的 6743
助记:bi-(两个)+parti-(=party:党派)+-san(名词后缀,表人)→两个党派的人→两党的；两派的

combine [kəm'baɪn] vt. 使组合；使结合；使合并 vt. 同时做(两件完全不同的事)；兼有(不同的特点或品质)n. 联合收割机(又作combine harvester)；联盟；集团 1455
助记:com-(共同；一起)+bi-(两个)+n(增减无影响)+e→将两个拿到一起→联合；结合
搭配:combine with...:与……联系在一起；与……结合

例句:Sad to say, this project has turned out to be mostly low-level findings about factual errors and spelling and grammar mistakes, combined with lots of head-scratching puzzlement about what in the world those readers really want.

遗憾的是,这个项目结果大多是一些底层的发现,比如事实性错误,拼写和语法错误；以及许多让人头疼的困惑:那些读者究竟想要什么东西？

阅读难点:turn out to be:结果是

head-scratching: 令人挠头的, 令人头疼的

in the world (=on earth): 到底；究竟

仿写例句:遗憾的是,他们研究的结果往往都是一些缺乏说服力的大学排名,以及很多令人头疼的困惑,比如到底其依据是什么？

Sad to say, their research has turned out to be mostly inconvincing college ranking, combined with lots of head-scratching puzzlements about what in the world the bases are.

![](images/4202c6c67bc34479f1fe9d8f92350c06b95c8846a3e29609702e1624aa80b824.jpg)

balance ['bæləns] n. 平衡；均衡[+ between] [+of]；余额；等量 vt.&vi. (使)保持平衡；使 [重要性、数量、价值或影响] 相抵 vt. 权衡；斟酌[+against]；结平(账目)1640

词源:balance最初的本意是“天平”。它源自古拉丁语bilanx,由bi(two,

两个)+lanx(pans,盘)构成,指的就是“由两个秤盘构成的天平”。后来,该词又逐渐衍生出“平衡”的比喻之意,再在财会领域中,由“财务平衡表的差值”而衍生出“余额”之意。
助记:bi-(两个)+ -lan-(=dish, plate:秤盘)+ce(名词后缀)→两个秤盘构成天平→平衡；均衡；使平衡；使相抵；权衡→在财务上,引申义为余额(财务平衡表的差值)
搭配:on balance:全面考虑之后,权衡利弊

strike/achieve/find a balance:达至/取得/找到平衡

keep/lose a balance: 保持/失去平衡

upset the balance: 破坏平衡

a good/healthy balance:适当的比例

the balance of nature:自然界的平衡

balance the budget: 使收支平衡

balance liberty against the security:在自由和国家安全之间做出权衡

![](images/289813edfedadc5e0f835577815e68fc59264127b8b381f56dda565c54f7b7b2.jpg)

biscuit ['bɪskɪt] n. 烘烤两次的干面包；小圆饼(干)8222
搭配:古代西方人在航海时,为了解决漫长的海上旅行的饮食问题,发明了一种制作干粮的方法,那就是将烘烤好的面包,回炉再烘烤一次,使其变干变脆。这样处理过的干面包就可以保存很长时间而不会变质腐烂,特别适合长时间的海上旅程。这种烘烤两次的干面包就是饼干biscuit的前身。英语单词biscuit源自法语biscuit,由bis-(=bi=twice:两次)+cuit(cooked,烘烤过的),字面意思就是“烘烤过两次的面包”。
搭配:take the biscuit:糟糕透顶

![](images/4c1134fe4d437496e6613c9bd91b4b3fea6a4559f2c3c8ec9a9969fc87bc662e.jpg)

与 biscuit 中地 cuit 一样, 词根 coc- 也有 to cook, to ripen 煎调, 成熟的含义。

词源:pekw

Proto-Indo-European root meaning "to cook, ripen."

It is the hypothetical source of/evidence for its existence is provided by: Sanskrit pakvah "cooked, ripe;" Avestan -paka- "cooked," Greek peptein "to cook, ripen, digest," pepon "ripe;" Latin coquere "to cook, prepare food, ripen, digest, turn over in the mind," Oscan popina "kitchen;" Lithuanian kepti "to bake, roast;" Old Church Slavonic pecenu "roasted;" Welsh poeth "cooked, baked, hot."
助记:pre-(=before:在前,早于)+coc(=to cook, ripen:烹调；成熟,词源同cook, cuisine。之前指代花或果实的成熟,后来用于比喻人的成熟)+ious(形容词后缀)→早熟的(maturing early)；智慧超前的(developed before the usual time)
搭配:a precocious child:早熟的儿童

display a precocious talent for music: 表现出不凡的音乐天赋

![](images/cf92978aa8dda4490bcbea0f97760145887474093e11739ea14da21006e7cac2.jpg)

与 biscuit, precocious 同样包含词根 coc-=cook, 表示烹调；成熟的单词还有:

cook [kʊk] vt.&vi. 烹调；烹制 n. 烹饪；(职业)厨师 1426

词源:“one whose occupation is the preparing and cooking of food,” Old English coc, from Vulgar Latin *cocus “cook,” from Latin coquus, from coquere “to cook, prepare food, ripen, digest, turn over in the mind” from PIE root *pekw- “to cook, ripen.”
搭配:cook dinner.: 做晚饭

be cooking: 密谋；秘密策划

be cooking with gas:如火如茶地进行；做得起劲

cook the books: 算改:伪造

cook sb's goose: 毁掉某人成功的机会

助记:cook(烹饪)+book(书籍)→烹饪书:烹饪菜谱

cooked [kukt] adj. 煮熟的 7648
搭配:steam cooked:蒸煮的

an electric cooker: 电炉灶

concoct [kən'kɒkt] vt. 虚构, 杜撰 (故事、借口等); 调制 (尤指食物或饮料)12756

concoction [kən'kɒkʃn] n. (古怪或少见的)调合物,调配品(尤指饮料或药物)14962

cuisine [kwɪ'zi:n] n. 烹饪；风味；(通常指昂贵的饭店中的)饭菜,菜肴 6498

词源: “manner or style of cooking,” 1786, from French cuisine “style of cooking,” originally “kitchen; cooking, cooked food” (12c.), from Late Latin cocina, earlier coquina “kitchen,” from Latin coquere “to cook,” from PIE root *pekw- “to cook, ripen.”
搭配:Italian cuisine:意大利式烹饪
the cuisine of Japan:日式烹调

culinary ['kʌlɪn(ə)ri] adj. 烹调的；食物的 7907

词源: 1630s, "of the kitchen;" 1650s, "pertaining to the art of cookery," from Latin culinarius "pertaining to the kitchen".
助记: culina (=kitchen, cooking stove, food: 厨房；厨灶；食物)+-ry(形容词后缀)→厨房的,有关烹饪艺术的→烹调的；食物的
搭配: culinary skills: 烹饪技能

culinary delights of Mexico: 墨西哥的美味

kiln [kɪln] vt. (砖, 石灰等的)窑; 炉; 干燥炉 16904
助记:来自古英语cyln, cylen “kiln, oven, furnace for drying or baking=炉子；窑炉” 来自拉丁语culina “kitchen, cooking stove=厨房；厨灶” coquere “to cook=做饭；烹调”.
搭配: rotary kiln:回转窑；回转炉
cement kiln:水泥窑

kitchen [ˈkɪtʃɪn; -tʃ(ə)n] n. 厨房 1055

词源:公元12世纪,“room in which food is cooked, part of a building fitted out for cooking,”含义为“烹饪食物的房间,适合烹饪的建筑物的一步分”。来自古英语cycene “kitchen=厨房”,来自古日耳曼kokina,也许借自民间拉丁文cocina(source also of French cuisine, Spanish cocina),拉丁文coquina的变体 “kitchen=厨房”,coquinus “of cooks”的阴性格,来自coquus “cook=厨师”,来自coquere “tocook=烹饪”。
助记:来源于拉丁词coquito,即“cook(厨师)。Coquito派生为coquina,cocina和cucina,古英语中变化为cycene,到了中古英语时期,又变作kitchene.
搭配: everything but the kitchen sink: 过多的东西；大量的东西
kitchen table: 餐桌

pumpkin ['pʌmpkɪn] n. 南瓜 6231

词源: 1640s, alteration of pompon, pumpion “melon, pumpkin” (1540s), from Middle French pompon, from Latin peponem (nominative pepo)“melon,” from Greek pepon “melon,” probably originally “cooked (by the sun),” hence “ripe;” from peptein “to cook”.
助记:pump (=melon: 瓜)+-kin(名词小词后缀)→南瓜
搭配:quarter the pumpkin:把南瓜一切四块

pumpkin pie: 南瓜(馅)饼

ricotta [rɪ'kɒtə] n. 羊奶乳清干酪 17985

词源:来自意大利语ricotta,字面含义为”recooked=再煮一便”。来自拉丁语recoquere的过去式的阴性形式,来自from re- (=again:再次)+coquere(to cook: 煮熟)→再煮一遍(奶酪需要煮两遍:一般生奶酪制作过程为,将纯奶放置在热处,使其发酵。当鲜奶有酸味后,再倒入锅中煮熬,待酸奶呈现出豆腐形状时,将其舀进纱布里,挤压除去水分。然后,把奶渣放进模具或木盘中,或挤压成形,或用刀划成方块,生奶酪就制做成功了。)

terra-cotta [,terə'kɒtə] n. 赤陶 15904
助记:1722, 来自意大利语terra cotta, 字面含义为 “cooked earth=被煮熟的土”, 来自terra (=earth: 土)+ cotta (=baked: 烤熟的)→烤熟的土→赤陶
搭配:plants in terracotta pots:赤陶花盆里的植物。

词根“di-”,“dia-”,“duo-”,“du-”=“two, double, twice”,也表示“两个”。

diploma [dr'pləʊmə] n. 结业证书, 考试证书[+in]; 毕业文凭, 学位证书 8618

词源: From Greek diploma "licence, chart," originally "paper folded double," from diploun "to double, fold over," from diploos "double" (see diplo-)+

-oma, suffix forming neuter nouns and nouns that indicate result of verbal action (see -oma).

词源: 英语单词diploma来自古希腊文diploma, 由diploun (对折)和oma (物品)构成, 字面意思就是 “可以对折的物品”, 最早指的是一种可以对折的铜片证书。在古罗马时期, 当一个蛮族雇佣军在罗马军队中服役25年 (海军26年)后, 即可获得罗马公民权利。为此, 罗马政府将为其提供一个凭证, 这个凭证就是所谓的Roman Military Diploma (罗马军事证书)。它由两片铜片构成, 里面刻有持有人的相关信息, 还有政府的烙印。铜片上留有小孔, 可以用铜丝穿过小孔, 把它们对折起来。拥有这种证书的蛮族人, 可以在罗马帝国的道路和边境自由通行。后来, diploma的词义扩展, 可以表示政府颁发的各种证书, 如大学的文凭。十八世纪, 法国人开始称呼他们与外国打交道的官员为diplomat, 也就是 “持有diploma的人”。
助记:diplo-(=double:对折)+-oma(名词后缀)→物品对折→证书:文凭
搭配:a diploma in catering:餐饮业资格证书

high school/college diploma:高中文凭/大学文凭

diploma 的派生词有 diplomacy, diplomat, diplomatic, diplomatically 等。

diplomacy [drɪ'pləʊməsi] n. 外交；外交手腕 5715
搭配:ping-pong diplomacy:乒乓外交

diplomat ['dɪpləmæt] n. 外交官；处事圆滑机敏的人 4968
搭配:French diplomats:法国外交官

diplomatic [dɪplə'mætɪk] adj. 外交的；圆通得体的 3978
搭配:dipomatic relations/ties:外交关系

diplomatically [ˌdɪpləˈmætɪkli] adv. 外交地 18140
搭配:resolve sth diplomatically:通过外交手段解决

double ['dʌb(ə)l] vt.&vi. 使加倍；翻倍 vi. 兼职 adj. 双的；成对的；双人的；双倍的；(酒类饮料)双份的 n. 双人房间；双份酒类饮料；一模一样的人；双打 pron. 两倍 predet 双倍的 2222
搭配:a double helping of ice cream:双份冰激凌
a pair of double doors:双扇门

on the double:快速地
bend double:弯腰的
see double:看到重影

doubly important:倍加重要

doubt [daut] n. 怀疑 vt. 怀疑 1920

Dyad is something that consists of two parts.

an operator which is the combination of two vectors.

单词 cycle 表示 “圈；周期；自行车”,其含义为 “revolve, move around, dwell: 旋转；循环；四处运动；居住。”

词源: 古词根kwel-。also *kwelə-, Proto-Indo-European root meaning "revolve, move round; sojourn, dwell." It is the hypothetical source of/evidence for its existence is provided by: Sanskrit cakram "circle, wheel," carati "he moves, wanders;" Avestan caraiti "applies himself," c'axra "chariot, wagon;" Greek kyklos "circle, wheel, any circular body, circular motion, cycle of events," polos "a round axis" (PIE *kw- becomes Greek p-before some vowels), polein "move around;" Latin colere "to frequent, dwell in, to cultivate, move around," cultus "tended, cultivated," hence

also "polished," colonus "husbandman, tenant farmer, settlers, colonist;" Lithuanian kelias "a road, a way;" Old Norse hvel, Old English hweol "wheel;" Old Church Slavonic kolo, Old Russian kolo, Polish koło, Russian koleso "a wheel."

cycle [ˈsɔɪk(ə)l] vi. 骑自行车 n. 周期；圈；自行车；骑自行车 2240
助记:n. cycl-(圆；圈)+e→圈；周期；自行车 vi. cycl+e→revolve in cycles, occur or recur in cycles: 转圈；出现圈或圈重复出现→骑自行车
搭配:the life cycle of the plant: 植物的生命周期

10 cycles per second: 每秒10圈

be ideal for cycling: 很适合骑自行车 cell cycle: 细胞周期

![](images/d8d57c7fb42cee75a2a5e7e659131727bf0582dc6a2a20f66ad6c6f82c374a01.jpg)

cycle 的派生词有 cyclical, cycling, cyclist, bicycle, recycle, recycled, recycling, recyclable 等。

cyclical ['sɪklɪk(ə)l] adj. 周期的；(乐曲)循环的 12890
搭配: the cyclical nature of the airline business: 航空业的周期性特征

cycling ['saɪklɪŋ] n. 骑自行车运动(或活动)8359
搭配:cycling shorts:自行车短运动裤 to go cycling:去骑自行车
